// Working state — deep clone so edits don't corrupt original
let D = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(ORIG));

// FERIADOS março 2026 — editável
const FERIADOS_BASE = ['2026-03-03','2026-03-04'];
function getFeriados(){try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cofen_feriados')||JSON.stringify(FERIADOS_BASE));}catch(e){return FERIADOS_BASE;}}
function setFeriados(arr){localStorage.setItem('cofen_feriados',JSON.stringify(arr));}

// ─ Config ─
const META_DEFAULT = 800000;
let meta = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('cofen_meta') || META_DEFAULT);
let overrideTotalRec = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('cofen_total') || '0');

const EQ={
  "COFEN MARILIA BRENDA":   {c:"#00A86B",bg:"#E6F7F1",ico:"🏙",sh:"Marília Brenda"},
  "COFEN BIRIGUI BRUNA":    {c:"#4776E6",bg:"#EEF2FF",ico:"💙",sh:"Birigui Bruna"},
  "COFEN STEPHANIE 2° TURNO":{c:"#F7971E",bg:"#FFF7ED",ico:"⭐",sh:"Stephanie 2°T"},
  "COFEN BIRIGUI LUCIANO":  {c:"#f953c6",bg:"#FDF2FF",ico:"💜",sh:"Birigui Luciano"},
  "ELITE":                  {c:"#FC5C7D",bg:"#FFF0F3",ico:"💎",sh:"Elite"},

};

const fR=v=>v.toLocaleString("pt-BR",{style:"currency",currency:"BRL"});
const fRK=v=>v>=1000?"R$ "+(v/1000).toFixed(1)+"K":fR(v);
const ini=n=>{const p=n.replace(/_/g," ").split(" ");return p.length>=2?(p[0][0]+p[1][0]).toUpperCase():n.slice(0,2).toUpperCase()};

// All operators sorted
let ALL = [];
function rebuildAll(){
  ALL = D.equipes.flatMap(e=>e.ops.map(o=>({...o,eq:e.name}))).sort((a,b)=>b.rec-a.rec);
}
rebuildAll();

// ── CALENDAR & DU ──
let DU = {total:20, passou:13, restam:7};

function buildCal(gridId){
  const now = new Date();
  const year = now.getFullYear(), month = now.getMonth();
  const today = now.getDate();
  const months = ["Janeiro","Fevereiro","Março","Abril","Maio","Junho",
    "Julho","Agosto","Setembro","Outubro","Novembro","Dezembro"];

  if(document.getElementById('cal-title'))
    document.getElementById('cal-title').textContent = months[month];
  if(document.getElementById('cal-year-txt'))
    document.getElementById('cal-year-txt').textContent = year + ' · Seg a Sex = Dia Útil';

  const firstDay = new Date(year,month,1).getDay(); // 0=sun
  const daysInMonth = new Date(year,month+1,0).getDate();
  const grid = document.getElementById(gridId);
  if(!grid) return;
  grid.innerHTML = '';

  const dayNames = ['Dom','Seg','Ter','Qua','Qui','Sex','Sáb'];
  dayNames.forEach((d,i)=>{
    const el=document.createElement('div');
    el.className='cal-dn'+(i===0||i===6?' we':'');
    el.textContent=d; grid.appendChild(el);
  });
  for(let i=0;i<firstDay;i++){
    const el=document.createElement('div');el.className='cal-day emp';grid.appendChild(el);
  }

  let duTotal=0,duPassed=0;
  for(let d=1;d<=daysInMonth;d++){
    const dt = new Date(year,month,d);
    const dow = dt.getDay();
    const iso = `${year}-${String(month+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(d).padStart(2,'0')}`;
    const isFeriado = getFeriados().includes(iso);
    const isWeekend = dow===0||dow===6;
    const duOv = getDUOverrides()[iso];
    const isWorkday = duOv===true ? true : duOv===false ? false : (!isWeekend && !isFeriado);
    const isManualUtil = duOv===true;
    const isToday = d===today;
    const isPast = d<today;

    if(isWorkday) duTotal++;
    if(isWorkday && (isPast||isToday)) duPassed++;

    let cls='cal-day';
    if(isManualUtil && isPast) cls+=' past'; // manual = verde
    else if(isManualUtil && isToday) cls+=' today';
    else if(isManualUtil) cls+=' fut'; // manual futuro
    else if(isWeekend) cls+=' wk';
    else if(isFeriado) cls+=' feria';
    else if(isToday) cls+=' today';
    else if(isPast) cls+=' past';
    else cls+=' fut';

    const el=document.createElement('div');
    el.className=cls;
    // Day number
    const dayNum=document.createElement('span');
    dayNum.textContent=d;
    el.appendChild(dayNum);
    // Event dots
    const evs=evGetByDate(iso);
    if(evs.length>0){
      const dots=document.createElement('div');
      dots.className='cal-ev-dots';
      evs.slice(0,4).forEach(ev=>{
        const dot=document.createElement('div');
        dot.className='cal-ev-dot';
        const ec=(EV_TIPOS[ev.tipo]||EV_TIPOS.lembrete).c;
        dot.style.background=isToday?'rgba(255,255,255,.85)':ec;
        dots.appendChild(dot);
      });
      el.appendChild(dots);
      el.classList.add('has-ev');
    }
    // Click handler (any non-empty, non-weekend day OR weekend with events)
    if(!cls.includes('emp') && !cls.includes('wk') || evs.length>0){
      el.style.cursor='pointer';
      el.onclick=(()=>{const di=iso;return()=>evOpenModal(di);})();
    } else if(cls.includes('wk')){
      el.style.cursor='pointer';
      el.onclick=(()=>{const di=iso;return()=>evOpenModal(di);})();
    }
    grid.appendChild(el);
  }

  DU.total=duTotal; DU.passou=duPassed; DU.restam=Math.max(0,duTotal-duPassed);
  // Update all DU displays
  ['du-total','du2-total'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=DU.total;});
  ['du-passou','du2-passou'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=DU.passou;});
  ['du-restam','du2-restam'].forEach(id=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=DU.restam;});
}

// ── EDITOR MANUAL DE DIAS ÚTEIS ──
// Estado dos overrides manuais: { '2026-03-03': true/false }
// true = forçar como útil, false = forçar como não-útil
function getDUOverrides(){try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cofen_du_overrides')||'{}');}catch(e){return {};}}
function setDUOverrides(obj){localStorage.setItem('cofen_du_overrides',JSON.stringify(obj));}

function buildDUManualGrid(){
  const now=new Date(), year=now.getFullYear(), month=now.getMonth();
  const daysInMonth=new Date(year,month+1,0).getDate();
  const overrides=getDUOverrides();
  const feriados=getFeriados();
  const grid=document.getElementById('du-manual-grid');
  if(!grid) return;
  grid.innerHTML='';
  let countUtil=0;
  for(let d=1;d<=daysInMonth;d++){
    const dt=new Date(year,month,d);
    const dow=dt.getDay();
    const iso=`${year}-${String(month+1).padStart(2,'0')}-${String(d).padStart(2,'0')}`;
    const baseUtil=dow>0&&dow<6&&!feriados.includes(iso);
    // override: true=forçar útil, false=forçar não-útil, undefined=automático
    const ov=overrides[iso];
    const isUtil=ov===true?true:ov===false?false:baseUtil;
    const isManual=ov!==undefined;
    if(isUtil) countUtil++;
    const dayNames=['D','S','T','Q','Q','S','S'];
    const btn=document.createElement('button');
    btn.title=iso+' — '+(isUtil?'Dia Útil':'Não Útil')+(isManual?' (manual)':' (auto)');
    btn.style.cssText=`border-radius:6px;border:none;cursor:pointer;padding:5px 2px;font-size:11px;
      font-weight:800;transition:all .2s;font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;
      background:${ov===true?'#FFF7ED':ov===false?'#FEF2F2':isUtil?'#D1FAE5':'#f1f5f9'};
      color:${ov===true?'#92400E':ov===false?'#B91C1C':isUtil?'#065F46':'#94a3b8'};
      border:1px solid ${ov===true?'#FCD34D':ov===false?'#FCA5A5':isUtil?'rgba(0,168,107,.2)':'transparent'}`;
    btn.innerHTML=`<span style="font-size:9px;display:block;opacity:.7">${dayNames[dow]}</span>${d}`;
    btn.onclick=()=>duToggleDay(iso);
    grid.appendChild(btn);
  }
  const el=document.getElementById('du-manual-count');
  if(el) el.textContent=countUtil+' dias úteis';
}

function duToggleDay(iso){
  const overrides=getDUOverrides();
  const now=new Date(), year=now.getFullYear(), month=now.getMonth();
  const [y,m,d]=iso.split('-').map(Number);
  const dt=new Date(y,m-1,d);
  const dow=dt.getDay();
  const feriados=getFeriados();
  const baseUtil=dow>0&&dow<6&&!feriados.includes(iso);
  const ov=overrides[iso];
  // Ciclo: auto → forçar oposto → auto
  if(ov===undefined) overrides[iso]=!baseUtil; // força oposto
  else delete overrides[iso]; // volta ao auto
  setDUOverrides(overrides);
  buildDUManualGrid();
}

function duApplyManual(){
  buildCal('cal-grid');
  buildCal('cal-grid2');
  initHero();
  toast('✅ Dias úteis atualizados!');
}

function duResetManual(){
  if(!confirm('Resetar para o calendário automático?')) return;
  localStorage.removeItem('cofen_du_overrides');
  buildDUManualGrid();
  buildCal('cal-grid');
  buildCal('cal-grid2');
  initHero();
  toast('↩ Dias úteis resetados para automático!');
}

// ── TOTAL REC (with override) ──
function getTotalRec(){
  return overrideTotalRec > 0
    ? overrideTotalRec
    : D.equipes.reduce((s,e)=>s+e.rec,0);
}

// ── INIT HERO & GERAL ──
function initHero(){
  const totalRec = getTotalRec();
  const totalHO  = totalRec * 0.25;
  const falta    = Math.max(0, meta - totalRec);
  const media    = DU.passou>0 ? totalRec/DU.passou : 0;
  const need     = DU.restam>0 ? falta/DU.restam : 0;
  const totalAc  = D.equipes.reduce((s,e)=>s+e.acordos,0);

  document.getElementById('h-total').textContent = fRK(totalRec);
  document.getElementById('h-ho').textContent    = fRK(totalHO);
  document.getElementById('h-falta').textContent = falta>0 ? fRK(falta) : '✅ Meta!';
  document.getElementById('h-falta').className   = 'hkpi-v '+(falta>0?'am':'ok');
  document.getElementById('h-meta-s').textContent= 'Meta: '+fRK(meta);
  document.getElementById('h-media').textContent = fRK(media);
  document.getElementById('h-du-s').textContent  = DU.passou+' D.U. passados';
  document.getElementById('h-need').textContent  = DU.restam>0 ? fRK(need) : '—';
  document.getElementById('h-restam-s').textContent = DU.restam+' D.U. restantes';
  document.getElementById('h-ac').textContent    = totalAc.toLocaleString('pt-BR');
  // Progress bar
  const pct = meta>0 ? Math.min(100, totalRec/meta*100) : 0;
  const barEl = document.getElementById('h-meta-bar');
  const pctEl = document.getElementById('h-meta-pct');
  if(barEl) setTimeout(()=>{barEl.style.width=pct.toFixed(1)+'%';},100);
  if(pctEl) pctEl.textContent = pct.toFixed(1)+'% da meta';
  if(barEl && pct>=100){ barEl.style.background='linear-gradient(90deg,#4ADE80,#00C97F)'; }
  else if(barEl && pct>=70){ barEl.style.background='linear-gradient(90deg,#FCD34D,#F59E0B)'; }
  else if(barEl){ barEl.style.background='linear-gradient(90deg,#FCA5A5,#EF4444)'; }
}

// ── CHARTS ──
let charts={};
function destroyC(id){if(charts[id]){charts[id].destroy();delete charts[id];}}

function mkGD(){
  destroyC('gd');
  const days=Object.keys(D.global.daily).map(Number).sort((a,b)=>a-b);
  const vals=days.map(d=>D.global.daily[d]);
  charts.gd=new Chart(document.getElementById('ch-gd').getContext('2d'),{
    type:'bar',
    data:{labels:days.map(d=>'D'+d),datasets:[{label:'Recebido',data:vals,
      backgroundColor:vals.map(v=>v>=30000?'rgba(0,168,107,.9)':v>=15000?'rgba(0,168,107,.6)':'rgba(0,168,107,.35)'),
      borderRadius:4,borderSkipped:false}]},
    options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,
      plugins:{legend:{display:false},tooltip:{callbacks:{label:ctx=>'R$ '+ctx.raw.toLocaleString('pt-BR',{minimumFractionDigits:0})}}},
      scales:{x:{grid:{display:false},ticks:{font:{size:9},color:'#7A8899'}},
        y:{grid:{color:'rgba(0,0,0,.05)'},ticks:{font:{size:9},color:'#7A8899',callback:v=>'R$'+v/1000+'K'}}}}
  });
}

function mkDist(){
  destroyC('dd');
  const colors=D.equipes.map(e=>EQ[e.name]?.c||'#888');
  charts.dd=new Chart(document.getElementById('ch-dist').getContext('2d'),{
    type:'doughnut',
    data:{labels:D.equipes.map(e=>EQ[e.name]?.sh||e.name),
      datasets:[{data:D.equipes.map(e=>e.rec),backgroundColor:colors,borderWidth:2,borderColor:'#fff'}]},
    options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,cutout:'68%',
      plugins:{legend:{display:false},tooltip:{callbacks:{label:ctx=>ctx.label+': '+fRK(ctx.raw)}}}}
  });
  const totalRec=getTotalRec();
  document.getElementById('dist-leg').innerHTML=D.equipes.map(e=>{
    const cfg=EQ[e.name]||{c:'#888',sh:e.name};
    const pct=(e.rec/totalRec*100).toFixed(1);
    return `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:7px">
      <div style="width:9px;height:9px;border-radius:2px;background:${cfg.c};flex-shrink:0"></div>
      <div style="flex:1;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:#3D4B5C;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap">${cfg.sh}</div>
      <div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:800;color:#1A2330">${pct}%</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

// TOP 5 list
function mkTop5(){
  const top5=ALL.slice(0,5);
  document.getElementById('top5-list').innerHTML=top5.map((op,i)=>{
    const cfg=EQ[op.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:op.eq};
    const medals=['🥇','🥈','🥉','4°','5°'];
    const pct=Math.round(op.rec/top5[0].rec*100);
    return `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:8px 10px;background:var(--g50);border-radius:var(--rm);cursor:pointer;transition:all .2s"
      onclick="openM('${op.name}')"
      onmouseover="this.style.background='var(--w)';this.style.boxShadow='var(--sh-md)'"
      onmouseout="this.style.background='var(--g50)';this.style.boxShadow=''">
      <div style="width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:8px;background:${cfg.c};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-weight:900;font-size:11px;color:#fff;flex-shrink:0">${ini(op.name)}</div>
      <div style="flex:1;min-width:0">
        <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:12px;color:#1A2330;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${medals[i]} ${op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div>
        <div style="background:var(--g200);border-radius:100px;height:3px;overflow:hidden;margin-top:4px">
          <div style="width:${pct}%;height:100%;border-radius:100px;background:${cfg.c}"></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:right;flex-shrink:0">
        <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:15px;color:${cfg.c};letter-spacing:.5px">${fR(op.rec)}</div>
        <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500)">HO: <strong style="color:var(--ok)">${fR(op.ho)}</strong></div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

// ── EDITOR ──
function buildOpEditor(){
  document.getElementById('inp-total').value = overrideTotalRec > 0 ? overrideTotalRec : '';
  document.getElementById('inp-meta').value  = meta;
  liveCalc();

  // Load saved op overrides
  const saved = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cofen_op_overrides')||'{}');

  document.getElementById('op-editor-list').innerHTML = ALL.map(op=>{
    const cfg=EQ[op.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:op.eq};
    const savedVal = saved[op.name] !== undefined ? saved[op.name] : op.rec;
    const isEdited = saved[op.name] !== undefined;
    return `<div class="op-row ${isEdited?'edited':''}" id="oprow-${op.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_')}">
      <div>
        <div class="op-name">${op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div>
        <div class="op-team" style="color:${cfg.c}">${cfg.sh}</div>
      </div>
      <input class="op-inp" type="number" id="opinp-${op.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_')}"
        value="${savedVal.toFixed(2)}" step="0.01" min="0"
        oninput="onOpInput('${op.name.replace(/'/g,"\\'")}',this)"
        placeholder="${op.rec.toFixed(2)}">
      <div id="opho-${op.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_')}"
        style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:14px;color:var(--ok);text-align:right;padding-right:4px">
        ${fR(savedVal*0.25)}
      </div>
      <button class="op-reset" onclick="resetOp('${op.name.replace(/'/g,"\\'")}')">↩</button>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function onOpInput(opName, inp){
  const safeId = opName.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_');
  const v = parseFloat(inp.value)||0;
  const ho = v*0.25;
  document.getElementById('opho-'+safeId).textContent = fR(ho);
  document.getElementById('oprow-'+safeId).classList.add('edited');
}

function applyOps(){
  const overrides = {};
  ALL.forEach(op=>{
    const safeId = op.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_');
    const inp = document.getElementById('opinp-'+safeId);
    if(!inp) return;
    const v = parseFloat(inp.value)||0;
    if(Math.abs(v - op.rec) > 0.01) overrides[op.name] = v;
  });

  // Apply to D
  D.equipes.forEach(eq=>{
    eq.ops.forEach(op=>{
      if(overrides[op.name] !== undefined){
        op.rec = overrides[op.name];
        op.ho  = op.rec * 0.25;
      }
    });
    // Recalc equipe totals
    eq.rec = eq.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.rec,0);
    eq.ho  = eq.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.ho,0);
  });

  localStorage.setItem('cofen_op_overrides', JSON.stringify(overrides));
  rebuildAll();
  refreshAll();
  toast('✅ '+Object.keys(overrides).length+' operadores atualizados!');
}

function resetOp(opName){
  const origEq = ORIG.equipes.find(e=>e.ops.some(o=>o.name===opName));
  const origOp = origEq?.ops.find(o=>o.name===opName);
  if(!origOp) return;

  const safeId = opName.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_');
  const inp = document.getElementById('opinp-'+safeId);
  if(inp) inp.value = origOp.rec.toFixed(2);
  document.getElementById('opho-'+safeId).textContent = fR(origOp.rec*0.25);
  document.getElementById('oprow-'+safeId).classList.remove('edited');
}

function resetOps(){
  D = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(ORIG));
  localStorage.removeItem('cofen_op_overrides');
  overrideTotalRec = 0;
  localStorage.removeItem('cofen_total');
  rebuildAll();
  buildOpEditor();
  refreshAll();
  fbPush('overrides', {});
  fbPush('meta', {total: 0, meta: META_DEFAULT});
  toast('↩ Todos os valores resetados e sincronizados!');
}

// ── LIVE CALC ──
function liveCalc(){
  const v = parseFloat(document.getElementById('inp-total').value)||0;
  const m = parseFloat(document.getElementById('inp-meta').value)||META_DEFAULT;
  const ho    = v*0.25;
  const falta = Math.max(0,m-v);
  const media = DU.passou>0 ? v/DU.passou : 0;
  const need  = DU.restam>0 ? falta/DU.restam : 0;

  document.getElementById('res-ho').textContent    = v>0 ? fR(ho) : '—';
  document.getElementById('res-falta').textContent = v>0 ? (falta>0?fR(falta):'✅ Meta!') : '—';
  document.getElementById('res-falta').className   = 'res-v '+(falta>0?'rd':'ok');
  document.getElementById('res-media').textContent = v>0 ? fR(media) : '—';
  document.getElementById('res-need').textContent  = v>0 && DU.restam>0 ? fR(need) : '—';
  document.getElementById('res-meta-lbl').textContent = 'Meta: '+fRK(m);
  document.getElementById('res-du-lbl').textContent   = DU.passou+' D.U. passados';
  document.getElementById('res-rest-lbl').textContent = DU.restam+' D.U. restam';
}

function applyTotal(){
  const v = parseFloat(document.getElementById('inp-total').value)||0;
  const m = parseFloat(document.getElementById('inp-meta').value)||META_DEFAULT;
  if(v>0) overrideTotalRec = v;
  meta = m;
  localStorage.setItem('cofen_meta',  m);
  localStorage.setItem('cofen_total', v);
  refreshAll();
  // Sincronizar para todos via Firebase (outros dispositivos) e BroadcastChannel (outras abas)
  fbPush('meta', {total: v, meta: m});
  syncBroadcast('meta_update', JSON.stringify({total: v, meta: m}));
  const syncMsg = fbDb && fbRoom ? '✅ Aplicado e sincronizado para todos!' : '✅ Total e meta aplicados!';
  toast(syncMsg);
}

function resetTotal(){
  overrideTotalRec = 0;
  meta = META_DEFAULT;
  localStorage.removeItem('cofen_total');
  localStorage.removeItem('cofen_meta');
  document.getElementById('inp-total').value = '';
  document.getElementById('inp-meta').value  = META_DEFAULT;
  liveCalc();
  refreshAll();
  // Sincronizar reset para todos
  fbPush('meta', {total: 0, meta: META_DEFAULT});
  syncBroadcast('meta_update', JSON.stringify({total: 0, meta: META_DEFAULT}));
  toast('↩ Resetado para valores originais!');
}

// ── EQUIPES PAGE ──
function mkEq(){
  const totalRec=getTotalRec();
  document.getElementById('eq-grid').innerHTML=D.equipes.map(eq=>{
    const cfg=EQ[eq.name]||{c:'#888',bg:'#eee',ico:'📌',sh:eq.name};
    const pct=(eq.rec/totalRec*100).toFixed(1);
    return `<div class="eq-card" style="--ec:${cfg.c}" onclick="openEq('${eq.name}')">
      <div class="eq-tip">Ver operadores →</div>
      <div class="eq-hdr">
        <div class="eq-ico" style="background:${cfg.bg}">${cfg.ico}</div>
        <div><div class="eq-nm">${cfg.sh}</div><div class="eq-op">${eq.n_op} operadores · ${eq.acordos} acordos</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="eq-kpis">
        <div class="eq-k"><div class="eq-k-l">Total Real</div><div class="eq-k-v" style="color:${cfg.c}">${fRK(eq.rec)}</div></div>
        <div class="eq-k"><div class="eq-k-l">HO (25%)</div><div class="eq-k-v">${fRK(eq.ho)}</div></div>
        <div class="eq-k"><div class="eq-k-l">Média/Op</div><div class="eq-k-v" style="color:#3B82F6">${fRK(eq.rec/eq.n_op)}</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="eq-bar-bg"><div class="eq-bar-f" style="width:${Math.min(100,parseFloat(pct))}%;background:${cfg.c}"></div></div>
      <div class="eq-hint"><span style="color:${cfg.c}">${pct}% do total</span><span>${fRK(eq.rec)}</span></div>
      ${(()=>{
        const metaEq = getMetaEquipe(eq.name);
        if(!metaEq) return '';
        const projEq = calcProjecao(eq.rec, metaEq);
        return '<div style="margin-top:8px;padding:7px 10px;border-radius:var(--r);background:'+projEq.color+'12;border:1px solid '+projEq.color+'30;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between">'
          +'<div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:var(--g700)">Projeção da equipe</div>'
          +'<div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:16px;color:'+projEq.color+'">'+projEq.pct.toFixed(0)+'%</div>'
          +'</div>';
      })()}
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function openEq(n){ go('ranking',document.querySelector('.tabs .tab:nth-child(4)')); rkFilter=n; mkRanking(); }

// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// META INDIVIDUAL POR OPERADOR
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
function getMetasOp(){ try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cofen_metas_op')||'{}');}catch(e){return {};} }
function setMetasOp(obj){ localStorage.setItem('cofen_metas_op', JSON.stringify(obj)); }
function getMetaOp(opName){ return getMetasOp()[opName]||0; }
function setMetaOp(opName, val){ const m=getMetasOp(); if(val>0) m[opName]=val; else delete m[opName]; setMetasOp(m); }

// Calcula projeção: meta * (DU_passados / DU_total) = meta esperada até hoje
// Se rec >= meta_esperada → projetando (verde). Cor por % da meta_esperada
function calcProjecao(rec, metaInd){
  if(!metaInd || metaInd<=0) return {pct:0, color:'var(--g300)', label:'Sem meta', status:'none'};
  const duTotal  = DU.total  || 1;
  const duPassou = DU.passou || 1;
  const metaEsperada = metaInd * (duPassou / duTotal);
  const pct = metaEsperada > 0 ? (rec / metaEsperada * 100) : 0;
  let color, status, label;
  if(pct >= 100){
    color='var(--ok)'; status='ok';
    label='✅ Projetando meta!';
  } else if(pct >= 80){
    color='var(--info)'; status='info';
    label='🔵 Projeção boa';
  } else if(pct >= 50){
    color='var(--warn)'; status='warn';
    label='⚠️ Atenção';
  } else {
    color='var(--danger)'; status='danger';
    label='🔴 Abaixo da meta';
  }
  // falta por dia útil restante
  const falta = Math.max(0, metaInd - rec);
  const needDay = DU.restam > 0 ? falta / DU.restam : 0;
  return {pct, color, status, label, metaEsperada, falta, needDay};
}

// ── RANKING ──
let rkFilter='all';
function mkRanking(){
  document.getElementById('fbtns').innerHTML=
    `<button class="fbtn ${rkFilter==='all'?'on':''}" onclick="setF('all',this)">🏆 Todos</button>`+
    D.equipes.map(eq=>{
      const cfg=EQ[eq.name]||{c:'#888',sh:eq.name};
      const on=rkFilter===eq.name;
      return `<button class="fbtn ${on?'on':''}" onclick="setF('${eq.name}',this)"
        style="${on?'border-color:'+cfg.c+';background:'+cfg.c+'15;color:'+cfg.c:''}">${cfg.sh}</button>`;
    }).join('');

  const list=rkFilter==='all'?ALL:ALL.filter(o=>o.eq===rkFilter);
  const maxV=list[0]?.rec||1;
  document.getElementById('rk-list').innerHTML=list.map((op,i)=>{
    const r=i+1,cfg=EQ[op.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:op.eq};
    const cls=r===1?'r1':r===2?'r2':r===3?'r3':'';
    const bp=Math.round(op.rec/maxV*100);
    // ── Meta individual + projeção ──
    const metaInd = getMetaOp(op.name);
    const projData = calcProjecao(op.rec, metaInd);
    const projCol  = projData.color;
    const projLabel = projData.label;
    const projPct   = projData.pct;

    return `<div class="rk-row ${cls}" style="animation-delay:${i*.025}s;--ra:${cfg.c}" onclick="openM('${op.name}')">
      <div class="r-pos">${r<=3?['🥇','🥈','🥉'][r-1]:r+'°'}</div>
      <div class="r-info">
        <div style="width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;flex-shrink:0;background:${cfg.c};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center">
        ${photoGet(op.name)?`<img src="${photoGet(op.name)}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover">`:`<span style="font-weight:900;font-size:11px;color:#fff">${ini(op.name)}</span>`}
      </div>
        <div><div class="r-n">${op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div><div class="r-t">${cfg.sh}</div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="r-bar-w">
        <div class="r-val">${fR(op.rec)}</div>
        <div class="r-bar-bg"><div class="r-bar-f" style="width:${bp}%;background:${cfg.c}"></div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="r-ho">HO: <b>${fR(op.ho)}</b></div>
      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:2px;min-width:0">
        ${metaInd>0 ? `<div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:13px;color:${projCol};letter-spacing:.3px">${fRK(metaInd)}</div>
        <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500);font-weight:600">${projLabel}</div>` : `<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g300);font-weight:600">—</div>`}
      </div>
      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:3px">
        ${metaInd>0 ? `<div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:16px;color:${projCol};letter-spacing:.5px">${projPct.toFixed(0)}%</div>
        <div style="background:var(--g100);border-radius:100px;height:4px;width:60px;overflow:hidden">
          <div style="width:${Math.min(100,projPct)}%;height:100%;border-radius:100px;background:${projCol};transition:width 1s"></div>
        </div>` : `<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g300)">—</div>`}
      </div>
      <div class="r-ac">${op.acordos}</div>
      <div class="r-ag">${op.n_ag>0?'+'+op.n_ag:'—'}</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function setF(eq,btn){
  rkFilter=eq;
  document.querySelectorAll('.fbtn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('on'));
  if(btn) btn.classList.add('on');
  mkRanking();
}

// ── DIÁRIO CHARTS ──
function mkDf(){
  destroyC('df');
  const days=Object.keys(D.global.daily).map(Number).sort((a,b)=>a-b);
  charts.df=new Chart(document.getElementById('ch-df').getContext('2d'),{
    type:'bar',
    data:{labels:days.map(d=>'Dia '+d),datasets:[{label:'PaguePlay',
      data:days.map(d=>D.global.daily[d]),
      backgroundColor:'rgba(0,168,107,.7)',borderRadius:5,borderSkipped:false}]},
    options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,
      plugins:{legend:{display:false}},
      scales:{x:{grid:{display:false},ticks:{font:{size:10}}},
        y:{grid:{color:'rgba(0,0,0,.05)'},ticks:{font:{size:10},callback:v=>'R$'+v/1000+'K'}}}}
  });
}

function mkDe(){
  destroyC('de');
  const days=Array.from({length:22},(_,i)=>i+1);
  const ds=D.equipes.map(eq=>{
    const cfg=EQ[eq.name]||{c:'#888',sh:eq.name};
    const dm={};
    eq.ops.forEach(op=>Object.entries(op.daily).forEach(([d,v])=>{dm[d]=(dm[d]||0)+v;}));
    return {label:cfg.sh,data:days.map(d=>dm[d]||0),
      backgroundColor:cfg.c+'99',borderColor:cfg.c,borderWidth:1,borderRadius:2,borderSkipped:false};
  });
  charts.de=new Chart(document.getElementById('ch-de').getContext('2d'),{
    type:'bar',data:{labels:days.map(d=>'D'+d),datasets:ds},
    options:{responsive:true,maintainAspectRatio:false,
      scales:{x:{stacked:true,grid:{display:false},ticks:{font:{size:9}}},
        y:{stacked:true,grid:{color:'rgba(0,0,0,.05)'},ticks:{font:{size:9},callback:v=>'R$'+v/1000+'K'}}},
      plugins:{legend:{position:'bottom',labels:{font:{size:10},boxWidth:10,boxHeight:10}}}}
  });
}

// ── MODAL ──
function openM(opName){
  const op=ALL.find(o=>o.name===opName);if(!op)return;
  const cfg=EQ[op.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:op.eq};
  currentModalOp = opName;
  renderModalPhoto(opName, cfg);
  document.getElementById('m-name').textContent=op.name.replace(/_/g,' ').toUpperCase();
  document.getElementById('m-team').textContent=cfg.sh||op.eq;
  const tier=op.rec>=20000?{cls:'ts',lbl:'⭐ S — Top'}:op.rec>=10000?{cls:'ta',lbl:'A — Alta'}:op.rec>=5000?{cls:'tb',lbl:'B — Boa'}:{cls:'tc',lbl:'C — Dev.'};
  const te=document.getElementById('m-tier');te.className='tier '+tier.cls;te.textContent=tier.lbl;

  // Meta individual + projeção no modal
  const metaIndModal = getMetaOp(opName);
  const projModal    = calcProjecao(op.rec, metaIndModal);

  document.getElementById('m-kpis').innerHTML=[
    {l:'Total Real',v:fR(op.rec),cls:'ok'},
    {l:'HO (25%)',v:fR(op.ho),cls:''},
    {l:'Acordos',v:op.acordos,cls:'info'},
    {l:'Real/Acordo',v:fR(op.acordos>0?op.rec/op.acordos:0),cls:'am'},
    {l:'Agend. Valor',v:fR(op.val_ag),cls:'info'},
  ].map(k=>`<div class="mk"><div class="mk-l">${k.l}</div><div class="mk-v ${k.cls}">${k.v}</div></div>`).join('')
  + (metaIndModal>0 ? `
    <div class="mk" style="border:1.5px solid ${projModal.color}22;background:${projModal.color}08">
      <div class="mk-l">Meta Individual</div>
      <div class="mk-v" style="color:${projModal.color}">${fRK(metaIndModal)}</div>
    </div>
    <div class="mk" style="border:1.5px solid ${projModal.color}22;background:${projModal.color}08">
      <div class="mk-l">Projeção Mês</div>
      <div class="mk-v" style="color:${projModal.color};font-size:18px">${projModal.pct.toFixed(0)}%</div>
      <div style="font-size:9px;color:${projModal.color};font-weight:700;margin-top:2px">${projModal.label}</div>
    </div>
    ${projModal.needDay>0?`<div class="mk" style="border:1.5px solid var(--warn)22;background:var(--warn)08">
      <div class="mk-l">Falta/DU</div>
      <div class="mk-v am">${fRK(projModal.needDay)}</div>
      <div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--g500);font-weight:600;margin-top:2px">${DU.restam} D.U. restam</div>
    </div>`:''}
  ` : '');

  // ── AG-BOX: foto do operador se disponível, senão agendamentos ──
  const opPhoto = photoGet(opName);
  if(opPhoto){
    document.getElementById('m-ag').innerHTML=`
      <div style="position:relative;border-radius:var(--rm);overflow:hidden;background:var(--g50);border:1px solid var(--g200);min-height:220px;display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:10px">
        <img src="${opPhoto}" style="width:100%;height:220px;object-fit:cover;object-position:top;display:block;border-radius:var(--rm)">
        <div style="position:absolute;bottom:0;left:0;right:0;background:linear-gradient(transparent,rgba(0,0,0,.7));padding:14px 12px 10px">
          <div style="font-weight:900;font-size:13px;color:#fff">${opName.replace(/_/g,' ').toUpperCase()}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.7);font-weight:600">${cfg.sh||op.eq}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="position:absolute;top:8px;right:8px;display:flex;gap:5px">
          <button onclick="photoUpload()"
            style="padding:4px 8px;border-radius:100px;border:none;background:rgba(0,0,0,.55);color:#fff;
            font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;font-weight:700;font-size:10px;cursor:pointer;backdrop-filter:blur(4px)">📷 Trocar</button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  } else {
    document.getElementById('m-ag').innerHTML=`
      <div style="position:relative;border-radius:var(--rm);overflow:hidden;background:${cfg.c}18;border:2px dashed ${cfg.c}55;min-height:220px;display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:10px;cursor:pointer"
        onclick="photoUpload()" title="Clique para adicionar foto">
        <div style="width:72px;height:72px;border-radius:50%;background:${cfg.c};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-weight:900;font-size:26px;color:#fff">${ini(opName)}</div>
        <div style="text-align:center">
          <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:800;color:${cfg.c}">📷 Adicionar Foto</div>
          <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--g500);font-weight:600;margin-top:3px">${opName.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500);margin-top:2px">Clique para fazer upload</div>
        </div>
        <div class="ag-n" style="position:absolute;top:10px;left:14px">${op.n_ag}</div>
        <div style="position:absolute;bottom:10px;left:14px">
          <div class="ag-it">Agendamentos Futuros</div>
          <div class="ag-is">Total: ${fR(op.val_ag)}</div>
          <div class="ag-is" style="color:var(--info);font-weight:700;margin-top:3px">${op.n_ag>0?'Boletos a vencer':'Sem agendamentos'}</div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  }

  // Eficiência real com dados de acordos
  const gerados  = op.gerados   || op.acordos || 0;
  const pagos    = op.pagos     || 0;
  const pendentes= op.pendentes || (gerados-pagos);
  const avista   = op.avista    || 0;
  const ate3d    = op.ate3dias  || 0;
  const mais3d   = op.mais3dias || 0;
  const efPct    = gerados>0 ? (pagos/gerados*100).toFixed(1) : '0';

  const ticket   = op.ticket || (pagos>0 ? op.rec/pagos : 0);
  // Agendamentos futuros
  const agFuturo = op.ag_futuro || {};
  const agTotal  = Object.values(agFuturo).reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0);

  document.getElementById('m-efic').innerHTML=`

        <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500)">acordos pagos (${efPct}%)</div>

    </div>

      <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;margin-bottom:4px">
        <span style="color:var(--g500)">Taxa de conversão</span>
        <span style="color:${parseFloat(efPct)>=40?'var(--ok)':parseFloat(efPct)>=20?'var(--warn)':'var(--danger)'}">${efPct}%</span>
      </div>
      <div style="background:var(--g200);border-radius:100px;height:6px;overflow:hidden">
        <div style="width:${efPct}%;height:100%;border-radius:100px;background:${parseFloat(efPct)>=40?'var(--ok)':parseFloat(efPct)>=20?'var(--warn)':'var(--danger)'}"></div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:6px;margin-bottom:8px">
      <div class="ef-row" style="flex-direction:column;align-items:flex-start;gap:2px">
        <span class="ef-l">📋 Pendentes</span>
        <span style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:20px;color:var(--warn)">${pendentes}</span>
      </div>
      <div class="ef-row" style="flex-direction:column;align-items:flex-start;gap:2px">
        <span class="ef-l">📅 Agendamentos</span>
        <span style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:20px;color:var(--info)">${agTotal}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
    <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:5px">
      <div class="ef-row"><span class="ef-l">🚀 Pago à vista</span><span class="ef-v ok">${avista} (${avPct}%)</span></div>
      <div class="ef-row"><span class="ef-l">⏱ Pago 1–3 dias</span><span class="ef-v am">${ate3d}</span></div>
      <div class="ef-row"><span class="ef-l">🐢 Pago +3 dias</span><span class="ef-v ${mais3d>gerados*0.3?'rd':''}"> ${mais3d}</span></div>
      <div class="ef-row"><span class="ef-l">🎫 Ticket Médio</span><span class="ef-v info">${fR(ticket)}</span></div>
      <div class="ef-row"><span class="ef-l">📆 Dias médio lig→pgto</span><span class="ef-v ${op.media_dias<=1?'ok':op.media_dias<=5?'am':'rd'}">${(op.media_dias||0).toFixed(1)} dias</span></div>
    </div>
    ${agTotal>0?`<div style="margin-top:8px;padding:8px 10px;background:rgba(59,130,246,.06);border:1px solid rgba(59,130,246,.2);border-radius:var(--r)">
      <div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:800;color:var(--info);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.8px;margin-bottom:6px">📅 Próximos Agendamentos</div>
      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:3px">
        ${agDates.map(([dt,n])=>`<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:11px;font-weight:700">
          <span style="color:var(--g700)">${new Date(dt+'T12:00:00').toLocaleDateString('pt-BR',{day:'2-digit',month:'2-digit'})}</span>
          <span style="color:var(--info)">${n} acordo${n>1?'s':''}</span>
        </div>`).join('')}
        ${Object.keys(agFuturo).length>5?`<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500);font-weight:600;margin-top:2px">+${Object.keys(agFuturo).length-5} outras datas</div>`:''}
      </div>
    </div>`:''}
    `;

  const days=Array.from({length:22},(_,i)=>i+1);
  const maxD=Math.max(...Object.values(op.daily),1);
  document.getElementById('m-daily').innerHTML=days.map(d=>{
    const v=op.daily[d]||0;
    const h=Math.round(v/maxD*100);
    return `<div class="db-w" title="Dia ${d}: ${fR(v)}">
      <div class="db" style="height:${h}%;background:${v>0?'linear-gradient(180deg,'+cfg.c+','+cfg.c+'88)':'#EFF2F5'}"></div>
      <div class="db-l">${d}</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');

  const tipos=op.tipos;const totT=Object.values(tipos).reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0);
  const tcols={"PIX":"#00A86B","CARTÃO DE CRÉDITO":"#3B82F6","BOLETO NEGOCIAÇÃO":"#F59E0B"};
  document.getElementById('m-tipos').innerHTML=Object.entries(tipos)
    .sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1])
    .map(([k,v])=>{const p=totT>0?Math.round(v/totT*100):0;
      return `<div class="tr">
        <div class="tr-n">${k}</div>
        <div class="tr-bg"><div class="tr-f" style="width:${p}%;background:${tcols[k]||cfg.c}"></div></div>
        <div class="tr-v">${fR(v)}</div>
      </div>`;}).join('');

  // ── Gráfico evolução semanal ──
  renderWeeklyChart(op);

  document.getElementById('mov').classList.add('on');
}

function closeM(e){
  if(e&&e.target!==document.getElementById('mov')&&!e.target.classList.contains('mclose'))return;
  document.getElementById('mov').classList.remove('on');
}

// ── TABS ──
function go(id,el){
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab').forEach(t=>t.classList.remove('on'));
  if(el)el.classList.add('on');
  ['geral','editor','equipes','ranking','diario','recdia','gestao','import','acordos'].forEach(p=>document.getElementById('pg-'+p).classList.remove('on'));
  document.getElementById('pg-'+id).classList.add('on');
  if(id==='geral'){mkGD();mkDist();buildDUManualGrid();}
  if(id==='editor') buildOpEditor();
  if(id==='ranking') mkRanking();
  if(id==='diario'){mkDf();mkDe();buildCal('cal-grid2');}
  if(id==='recdia') rdInit();
  if(id==='gestao') gestaoInit();
  if(id==='import') importInit();
  if(id==='acordos') acordosInit();
}

// ── REFRESH ALL ──
function refreshAll(){
  rebuildAll();
  initHero();
  if(document.getElementById('pg-geral').classList.contains('on')){mkGD();mkDist();mkTop5();}
  if(document.getElementById('pg-equipes').classList.contains('on')) mkEq();
  if(document.getElementById('pg-ranking').classList.contains('on')) mkRanking();
}

// ── TOAST ──
function toast(msg){const t=document.getElementById('toast');t.textContent=msg;t.classList.add('on');setTimeout(()=>t.classList.remove('on'),3000);}

// ── CLOCK ──
function tick(){
  const now=new Date();
  const hms=[now.getHours(),now.getMinutes(),now.getSeconds()].map(n=>String(n).padStart(2,'0')).join(':');
  const dmy=now.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR',{weekday:'long',day:'2-digit',month:'2-digit',year:'numeric'});
  document.getElementById('clk').textContent=hms;
  document.getElementById('dt').textContent=dmy;
}

// ── LOAD SAVED OVERRIDES ON START ──
function loadSavedOverrides(){
  const savedOps = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cofen_op_overrides')||'{}');
  if(Object.keys(savedOps).length>0){
    D.equipes.forEach(eq=>{
      eq.ops.forEach(op=>{
        if(savedOps[op.name]!==undefined){
          op.rec=savedOps[op.name];
          op.ho=op.rec*0.25;
        }
      });
      eq.rec=eq.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.rec,0);
      eq.ho=eq.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.ho,0);
    });
    rebuildAll();
  }
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// RECEBIMENTO DO DIA — LÓGICA COMPLETA
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
function rdTodayKey(){
  const d=new Date();
  return 'cofen_rd_'+d.getFullYear()+'_'+(d.getMonth()+1)+'_'+d.getDate();
}
function rdGetSaved(){try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(rdTodayKey())||'{}')}catch(e){return {}}}
function rdSetSaved(map){localStorage.setItem(rdTodayKey(),JSON.stringify(map))}
function rdSumToday(){return Object.values(rdGetSaved()).reduce((s,v)=>s+(parseFloat(v)||0),0)}
function rdAtivos(){return Object.values(rdGetSaved()).filter(v=>(parseFloat(v)||0)>0).length}

function rdUpdateKPIs(){
  const hoje=rdSumToday(), hojeHO=hoje*0.25;
  const baseRec=getTotalRec(), accRec=baseRec+hoje, accHO=accRec*0.25;
  const ativos=rdAtivos();
  const metaDia=parseFloat(document.getElementById('rd-meta-dia')?.value||30680);
  const pct=metaDia>0?Math.min(100,hoje/metaDia*100):0;
  const falta=Math.max(0,metaDia-hoje);

  const s=(id,v)=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=v};
  s('rd-hoje-total',fR(hoje)); s('rd-hoje-ho',fR(hojeHO));
  s('rd-total-acc',fR(accRec)); s('rd-ho-acc',fR(accHO));
  s('rd-ativos',ativos);

  const bar=document.getElementById('rd-meta-bar');
  if(bar) bar.style.width=pct+'%';
  s('rd-meta-pct-lbl',pct.toFixed(1)+'% da meta diária');
  s('rd-meta-falta-lbl',falta>0?'Falta '+fR(falta):'✅ Meta do dia batida!');

  let tBase=0,tHO=0,tHoje=0;
  const saved=rdGetSaved();
  ALL.forEach(op=>{tBase+=op.rec;tHO+=op.ho;tHoje+=parseFloat(saved[op.name]||0);});
  s('rd-rod-base',fR(tBase)); s('rd-rod-ho',fR(tHO));
  s('rd-rod-hoje',fR(tHoje)); s('rd-rod-total',fR(tBase+tHoje));

  const now=new Date();
  const ds=now.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR',{weekday:'long',day:'2-digit',month:'long',year:'numeric'});
  s('rd-data-hoje',ds.charAt(0).toUpperCase()+ds.slice(1));
  rdRenderEqBreakdown();
}

function rdUpdateMeta(){rdUpdateKPIs()}

function rdOnInput(opName,inp){
  const v=parseFloat(inp.value)||0;
  const safeId=opName.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_');
  const op=ALL.find(o=>o.name===opName);
  const base=op?op.rec:0;
  const hojeHOEl=document.getElementById('rd-hojeho-'+safeId);
  const totalEl=document.getElementById('rd-totalhoje-'+safeId);
  if(hojeHOEl) hojeHOEl.textContent=fR(v*0.25);
  if(totalEl){
    totalEl.textContent=fR(base+v);
    totalEl.style.color=v>0?'var(--pp)':'var(--g500)';
  }
  const row=document.getElementById('rdrow-'+safeId);
  if(row) row.style.background=v>0?'#F0FDF4':'';
  const inpEl=document.getElementById('rdinp-'+safeId);
  if(inpEl) inpEl.style.borderColor=v>0?'var(--pp)':'var(--g200)';
  const map=rdGetSaved();
  if(v>0) map[opName]=v; else delete map[opName];
  rdSetSaved(map);
  rdUpdateKPIs();
}

// ── active sub-tab ──
let rdActiveEq='geral';

function rdBuildSubTabs(){
  const bar=document.getElementById('rd-subtabs');
  if(!bar) return;
  while(bar.children.length>1) bar.removeChild(bar.lastChild);
  const saved=rdGetSaved();
  D.equipes.forEach(eq=>{
    const cfg=EQ[eq.name]||{c:'#888',sh:eq.name};
    const hojeEq=eq.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+(parseFloat(saved[o.name]||0)),0);
    const isOn=rdActiveEq===eq.name;
    const tab=document.createElement('div');
    tab.className='rd-stab'+(isOn?' on':'');
    tab.dataset.eq=eq.name;
    tab.onclick=function(){rdSwitchTab(eq.name,this);};
    tab.style.cssText=`padding:11px 16px;font-weight:800;font-size:12px;cursor:pointer;
      white-space:nowrap;transition:all .2s;border-bottom:2px solid transparent;margin-bottom:-2px;
      color:${isOn?cfg.c:'var(--g500)'};border-bottom-color:${isOn?cfg.c:'transparent'};
      background:${isOn?cfg.c+'18':'transparent'}`;
    tab.innerHTML=cfg.ico+' '+cfg.sh+(hojeEq>0
      ?` <span style="font-size:10px;background:${cfg.c};color:#fff;padding:1px 7px;border-radius:100px;margin-left:4px">+${fRK(hojeEq)}</span>`
      :'');
    bar.appendChild(tab);
  });
}

function rdSwitchTab(eqName,el){
  rdActiveEq=eqName;
  const kpiBar=document.getElementById('rd-eq-kpi-bar');
  if(kpiBar) kpiBar.style.display=eqName==='geral'?'none':'block';
  const rodLbl=document.getElementById('rd-rod-label');
  if(rodLbl) rodLbl.textContent=eqName==='geral'?'💰 TOTAL GERAL':'💰 '+(EQ[eqName]?.sh||eqName).toUpperCase();
  rdRender();
}

function rdUpdateEqKpis(eqName){
  if(eqName==='geral') return;
  const eq=D.equipes.find(e=>e.name===eqName); if(!eq) return;
  const cfg=EQ[eqName]||{c:'#888'};
  const saved=rdGetSaved();
  const hojeEq=eq.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+(parseFloat(saved[o.name]||0)),0);
  const totalEq=eq.rec+hojeEq;
  const s=(id,v,col)=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e){e.textContent=v;if(col)e.style.color=col;}};
  s('eq-kpi-base',fR(eq.rec));
  s('eq-kpi-hoje',hojeEq>0?fR(hojeEq):'R$ 0,00',hojeEq>0?cfg.c:'var(--g300)');
  s('eq-kpi-total',fR(totalEq),cfg.c);
  s('eq-kpi-ho',fR(totalEq*0.25));
}

function rdRender(){
  const saved=rdGetSaved();
  const isGeral=rdActiveEq==='geral';
  const list=isGeral?ALL:ALL.filter(o=>o.eq===rdActiveEq);

  document.getElementById('rd-list').innerHTML=list.map(op=>{
    const cfg=EQ[op.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:op.eq};
    const sid=op.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_');
    const vHoje=parseFloat(saved[op.name]||0);
    const hasVal=vHoje>0;
    const histKey=rdTodayKey()+'_hist_'+sid;
    let hist=[]; try{hist=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(histKey)||'[]')}catch{}
    const histHtml=hist.slice(-3).map(h=>`<span style="font-size:9px;color:var(--g500)">${h.hora}</span><span style="font-size:9px;color:var(--pp);font-weight:800;margin-left:2px">+${fR(h.v)}</span>`).join(' &nbsp;');
    return `<div id="rdrow-${sid}"
      style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:32px 1fr 130px 110px 145px 130px 130px;
      gap:8px;align-items:center;padding:9px 18px;
      border-bottom:1px solid var(--g100);transition:background .2s;
      ${hasVal?'background:#FFFDF5':''}">
      <div style="width:28px;height:28px;border-radius:7px;background:${cfg.c};
        display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-weight:900;font-size:10px;color:#fff">${ini(op.name)}</div>
      <div>
        <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:12px;color:var(--g900);white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div>
        ${isGeral?`<div style="font-size:10px;color:${cfg.c};font-weight:700">${cfg.sh}</div>`:''}
        ${histHtml?`<div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:3px;margin-top:2px">${histHtml}</div>`:''}
      </div>
      <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:13px;color:var(--g700);text-align:right">${fR(op.rec)}</div>
      <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:13px;color:var(--ok);text-align:right">${fR(op.ho)}</div>
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:flex-end;gap:4px">
        <div style="position:relative">
          <span style="position:absolute;left:6px;top:50%;transform:translateY(-50%);
            font-size:9px;font-weight:700;color:var(--g500);pointer-events:none">R$</span>
          <input type="number" id="rdinp-${sid}"
            value="" placeholder="0,00" step="0.01" min="0"
            style="width:95px;background:#FFFBEB;border:1.5px solid #FCD34D;
            border-radius:var(--rm);padding:7px 5px 7px 20px;
            font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;font-size:12px;font-weight:800;color:var(--g900);
            outline:none;text-align:right;transition:all .2s"
            onfocus="this.style.borderColor='#F59E0B';this.style.boxShadow='0 0 0 3px rgba(245,158,11,.15)'"
            onblur="this.style.boxShadow=''"
            onkeydown="if(event.key==='Enter')rdAddAgora('${op.name.replace(/'/g,"\\'")}')">
        </div>
        <button onclick="rdAddAgora('${op.name.replace(/'/g,"\\'")}');"
          style="padding:6px 8px;border-radius:var(--r);border:none;cursor:pointer;
          background:linear-gradient(135deg,#F59E0B,#F97316);color:#fff;
          font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;font-weight:800;font-size:10px;white-space:nowrap">
          +Add
        </button>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:right">
        <div id="rd-hoje-acum-${sid}" style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:14px;
          color:${hasVal?'#F97316':'var(--g300)'};letter-spacing:.5px">
          ${hasVal?'+'+fR(vHoje):'—'}
        </div>
        <div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--g500);font-weight:600">acum. hoje</div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:right">
        <div id="rd-totalhoje-${sid}" style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:15px;
          color:${hasVal?cfg.c:'var(--g500)'};letter-spacing:.5px">${fR(op.rec+vHoje)}</div>
        <div id="rd-hojeho-${sid}" style="font-size:10px;color:var(--ok);font-weight:700">HO: ${fR((op.rec+vHoje)*0.25)}</div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');

  let tBase=0,tHO=0,tHoje=0;
  list.forEach(op=>{tBase+=op.rec;tHO+=op.ho;tHoje+=parseFloat(saved[op.name]||0);});
  const s2=(id,v)=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=v};
  s2('rd-rod-base',fR(tBase)); s2('rd-rod-ho',fR(tHO));
  s2('rd-rod-hoje',fR(tHoje)); s2('rd-rod-total',fR(tBase+tHoje));
  if(rdActiveEq!=='geral') rdUpdateEqKpis(rdActiveEq);
  rdBuildSubTabs();
  rdUpdateKPIs();
}

function rdAddAgora(opName){
  const sid=opName.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_');
  const inp=document.getElementById('rdinp-'+sid);
  if(!inp) return;
  const v=parseFloat(inp.value||0);
  if(!v||v<=0){ toast('⚠️ Digite um valor maior que zero'); return; }
  const map=rdGetSaved();
  map[opName]=(parseFloat(map[opName]||0))+v;
  rdSetSaved(map);
  // Histórico
  const histKey=rdTodayKey()+'_hist_'+sid;
  let hist=[]; try{hist=JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(histKey)||'[]')}catch{}
  const now=new Date();
  hist.push({v,hora:now.toLocaleTimeString('pt-BR',{hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'})});
  localStorage.setItem(histKey,JSON.stringify(hist));
  inp.value='';
  const op=ALL.find(o=>o.name===opName);
  const cfg=EQ[op?.eq||'']||{c:'var(--pp)'};
  const vHoje=parseFloat(map[opName]||0);
  const acumEl=document.getElementById('rd-hoje-acum-'+sid);
  const totalEl=document.getElementById('rd-totalhoje-'+sid);
  const hojehoEl=document.getElementById('rd-hojeho-'+sid);
  const row=document.getElementById('rdrow-'+sid);
  if(acumEl){acumEl.textContent='+'+fR(vHoje);acumEl.style.color='#F97316';}
  if(totalEl){totalEl.textContent=fR((op?.rec||0)+vHoje);totalEl.style.color=cfg.c;}
  if(hojehoEl) hojehoEl.textContent='HO: '+fR(((op?.rec||0)+vHoje)*0.25);
  if(row) row.style.background='#FFFDF5';
  rdUpdateKPIs();
  toast('💰 +'+fR(v)+' adicionado a '+opName.replace(/_/g,' '));
  try{ rdBC&&rdBC.postMessage({type:'rd',key:rdTodayKey(),data:map}); }catch{}
}


function rdSave(){toast('💾 Salvo automaticamente!');}

function rdClearDay(){
  if(!confirm('Zerar todos os valores do dia?\nEsta ação não pode ser desfeita.')) return;
  localStorage.removeItem(rdTodayKey());
  fbPush('rd', {});
  rdRender();
  toast('🗑 Dia zerado!');
}

function rdRenderEqBreakdown(){
  const saved=rdGetSaved();
  const el=document.getElementById('rd-eq-breakdown');
  if(!el) return;
  el.innerHTML=D.equipes.map((eq,idx)=>{
    const cfg=EQ[eq.name]||{c:'#888',bg:'#eee',ico:'📌',sh:eq.name};
    const baseRec=eq.rec,baseHO=eq.ho;
    const hojeRec=eq.ops.reduce((s,op)=>s+(parseFloat(saved[op.name]||0)),0);
    const totalRec=baseRec+hojeRec,totalHO=totalRec*0.25;
    const isLast=(idx+1)%3===0||idx===D.equipes.length-1;
    const bR=!isLast?'border-right:1px solid var(--g200);':'';
    const bB=idx<D.equipes.length-3?'border-bottom:1px solid var(--g200);':'';
    return `<div style="padding:14px 16px;${bR}${bB}">
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;margin-bottom:10px">
        <div style="width:30px;height:30px;border-radius:8px;background:${cfg.bg};
          display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:16px">${cfg.ico}</div>
        <div><div style="font-weight:800;font-size:12px;color:var(--g900)">${cfg.sh}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500);font-weight:600">${eq.n_op} op.</div></div>
        <button onclick="rdSwitchToEq('${eq.name}')"
          style="margin-left:auto;font-size:10px;color:${cfg.c};background:${cfg.c}14;
          border:1px solid ${cfg.c}44;border-radius:100px;padding:3px 8px;
          font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer">Editar →</button>
      </div>
      <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:5px">
        <div style="background:var(--g50);border-radius:var(--r);padding:7px 9px">
          <div style="font-size:9px;font-weight:700;color:var(--g500);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.6px;margin-bottom:2px">Base</div>
          <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:14px;color:var(--g700)">${fRK(baseRec)}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="background:${hojeRec>0?'#F0FDF4':'var(--g50)'};border-radius:var(--r);padding:7px 9px;
          border:${hojeRec>0?'1px solid rgba(0,168,107,.2)':'none'}">
          <div style="font-size:9px;font-weight:700;color:${hojeRec>0?'var(--ok)':'var(--g500)'};text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.6px;margin-bottom:2px">⚡ Hoje</div>
          <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:14px;color:${hojeRec>0?cfg.c:'var(--g300)'}">${hojeRec>0?fRK(hojeRec):'R$ 0'}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="background:var(--g50);border-radius:var(--r);padding:7px 9px">
          <div style="font-size:9px;font-weight:700;color:var(--g500);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.6px;margin-bottom:2px">HO Base</div>
          <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:14px;color:var(--ok)">${fRK(baseHO)}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="background:var(--g50);border-radius:var(--r);padding:7px 9px">
          <div style="font-size:9px;font-weight:700;color:var(--g500);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.6px;margin-bottom:2px">Total</div>
          <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:14px;color:${cfg.c};font-weight:800">${fRK(totalRec)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function rdSwitchToEq(eqName){
  // Switch sub-tab to that equipe
  go('recdia', document.querySelector('.tabs .tab:nth-child(6)'));
  rdActiveEq=eqName;
  const kpiBar=document.getElementById('rd-eq-kpi-bar');
  if(kpiBar) kpiBar.style.display='block';
  const rodLbl=document.getElementById('rd-rod-label');
  if(rodLbl) rodLbl.textContent='💰 '+(EQ[eqName]?.sh||eqName).toUpperCase();
  rdRender();
}

function rdInit(){
  rdActiveEq='geral';
  const kpiBar=document.getElementById('rd-eq-kpi-bar');
  if(kpiBar) kpiBar.style.display='none';
  rdBuildSubTabs();
  rdRender();
  rdRenderEqBreakdown();
}


// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// GESTÃO DE EQUIPES
// ══════════════════════════════════════════


// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// METAS INDIVIDUAIS POR OPERADOR — GESTÃO
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
let metaOpFilterEq = 'all';

function metaOpInit(){
  // Build equipe filter buttons
  const fb = document.getElementById('meta-op-fbtns');
  if(fb){
    const eqs = ['all', ...D.equipes.map(e=>e.name)];
    fb.innerHTML = eqs.map(eq=>{
      const cfg = eq==='all' ? {sh:'Todos',c:'var(--pp)'} : (EQ[eq]||{sh:eq,c:'#888'});
      const on  = metaOpFilterEq===eq;
      return '<button onclick="metaOpSetEq(\''+eq+'\')"'
        +' style="padding:6px 14px;border-radius:var(--rm);border:1.5px solid '+(on?cfg.c:'var(--g200)')+';'
        +'background:'+(on?cfg.c+'18':'var(--w)')+';color:'+(on?cfg.c:'var(--g500)')+';'
        +'font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;font-weight:800;font-size:11px;cursor:pointer;transition:all .2s">'
        +cfg.sh+'</button>';
    }).join('');
  }
  metaOpRender();
}

function metaOpSetEq(eq){
  metaOpFilterEq = eq;
  metaOpInit();
}

function metaOpRender(){
  const list_div = document.getElementById('meta-op-list');
  if(!list_div) return;
  const saved = getMetasOp();
  const list  = metaOpFilterEq==='all' ? ALL : ALL.filter(o=>o.eq===metaOpFilterEq);

  list_div.innerHTML = list.map(op=>{
    const cfg     = EQ[op.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:op.eq};
    const metaInd = saved[op.name]||0;
    const proj    = calcProjecao(op.rec, metaInd);
    const safeId  = op.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_');
    const barW    = metaInd>0 ? Math.min(100, op.rec/metaInd*100).toFixed(1) : 0;
    const avatarHtml = photoGet(op.name)
      ? `<img src="${photoGet(op.name)}" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover">`
      : ini(op.name);

    return `<div id="metaop-row-${safeId}"
      style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:36px 1fr 180px 160px;gap:10px;
      align-items:center;padding:9px 12px;border-radius:var(--rm);
      border:1px solid var(--g200);background:${metaInd>0?'var(--g50)':'var(--w)'}">
      <div style="width:32px;height:32px;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden;background:${cfg.c};
        display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-weight:900;font-size:11px;color:#fff">
        ${avatarHtml}
      </div>
      <div style="min-width:0">
        <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:12px;color:var(--g900);white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div>
        <div style="font-size:10px;color:${cfg.c};font-weight:700">${cfg.sh}</div>
        ${metaInd>0?`<div style="background:var(--g200);border-radius:100px;height:3px;overflow:hidden;margin-top:4px">
          <div style="width:${barW}%;height:100%;border-radius:100px;background:${proj.color};transition:width 1s"></div>
        </div>`:''}
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:center">
        ${metaInd>0
          ? `<div style="font-size:20px;font-weight:900;color:${proj.color};line-height:1">${proj.pct.toFixed(0)}%</div>
             <div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:${proj.color};margin-top:2px">${proj.label}</div>
             ${proj.needDay>0?`<div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--g500)">Falta: ${fRK(proj.needDay)}/DU</div>`:''}`
          : '<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g300)">Sem meta</div>'
        }
      </div>
      <div>
        <input type="number" id="metainp-${safeId}"
          value="${metaInd||''}" placeholder="Meta R$" step="100" min="0"
          style="width:120px;background:var(--w);border:1.5px solid var(--g200);border-radius:var(--rm);
          padding:7px 10px;font-size:13px;font-weight:800;color:var(--g900);outline:none;text-align:right;
          border-color:${metaInd>0?proj.color:'var(--g200)'}">
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function metaOpSave(){
  const saved = getMetasOp();
  ALL.forEach(op=>{
    const safeId = op.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_');
    const inp    = document.getElementById('metainp-'+safeId);
    if(!inp) return;
    const val = parseFloat(inp.value)||0;
    if(val>0) saved[op.name]=val; else delete saved[op.name];
  });
  setMetasOp(saved);
  fbPush('metas_op', saved);
  metaOpRender();
  if(document.getElementById('pg-ranking').classList.contains('on')) mkRanking();
  toast('✅ Metas individuais salvas e sincronizadas!');
}

function metaOpFillFromTeam(){
  const teamMetas = gGetMetas();
  const saved     = getMetasOp();
  D.equipes.forEach(eq=>{
    const tMeta = teamMetas[eq.name]||0;
    if(!tMeta) return;
    const nOps = eq.ops.length||1;
    const perOp = Math.round(tMeta / nOps / 100)*100;
    eq.ops.forEach(op=>{ saved[op.name] = perOp; });
  });
  setMetasOp(saved);
  metaOpRender();
  toast('⚡ Metas distribuídas igualmente por operador!');
}

// Storage key for manual additions / moves
function gGetOverrides(){ try{ return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cofen_gestao')||'{}'); }catch(e){return {};} }
function gSetOverrides(obj){ localStorage.setItem('cofen_gestao', JSON.stringify(obj)); }

// Get metas salvas
function gGetMetas(){ try{ return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cofen_metas_eq')||'{}'); }catch(e){return {};} }
function gSetMetas(obj){ localStorage.setItem('cofen_metas_eq', JSON.stringify(obj)); }

// ── SUB-TAB SWITCH ──
function gTab(id, el){
  document.querySelectorAll('.gtab').forEach(t=>{
    t.style.color='var(--g500)';
    t.style.borderBottomColor='transparent';
    t.style.background='transparent';
    t.classList.remove('on');
  });
  el.style.color='var(--pp)';
  el.style.borderBottomColor='var(--pp)';
  el.style.background='var(--ppl)';
  el.classList.add('on');
  document.querySelectorAll('.gsub').forEach(s=>s.style.display='none');
  document.getElementById('gsub-'+id).style.display='block';
  if(id==='mover') gestaoMoverInit();
  if(id==='metas') gestaoMetasInit();
  if(id==='novo')  gestaoNovoInit();
  if(id==='meta-op') metaOpInit();
  if(id==='fotos') fotosInit();
  if(id==='fotos') fotosInit();
}

// ── INIT ──
function gestaoInit(){
  gestaoMoverInit();
  gestaoMetasInit();
  gestaoNovoInit();
  fotosInit();
  metaOpInit();
}

function gestaoMoverInit(){
  // Populate operator select
  const selOp = document.getElementById('mv-op');
  const curVal = selOp.value;
  selOp.innerHTML = '<option value="">— Selecione o operador —</option>' +
    [...ALL].sort((a,b)=>a.name.localeCompare(b.name)).map(op=>{
      const eq = EQ[op.eq]||{sh:op.eq};
      return `<option value="${op.name}">${op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')} — ${eq.sh}</option>`;
    }).join('');
  if(curVal) selOp.value = curVal;

  // Populate equipe select
  const selEq = document.getElementById('mv-eq');
  selEq.innerHTML = '<option value="">— Selecione a equipe —</option>' +
    D.equipes.map(eq=>{
      const cfg = EQ[eq.name]||{sh:eq.name};
      return `<option value="${eq.name}">${cfg.ico||''} ${cfg.sh}</option>`;
    }).join('');

  // Render equipe composition list
  renderMvEqList();
  mvPreview();
}

function mvPreview(){
  const opName = document.getElementById('mv-op').value;
  const eqName = document.getElementById('mv-eq').value;
  const prev   = document.getElementById('mv-preview');
  if(!opName){ prev.style.display='none'; return; }
  const op  = ALL.find(o=>o.name===opName);
  const cfg = EQ[op?.eq]||{sh:op?.eq||'—'};
  const nCfg = eqName ? (EQ[eqName]||{sh:eqName}) : null;
  prev.style.display = 'block';
  document.getElementById('mv-from').innerHTML = `<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500);margin-bottom:3px">Equipe atual</div><strong style="color:${cfg.c||'#888'}">${cfg.sh}</strong>`;
  document.getElementById('mv-to').innerHTML = nCfg
    ? `<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500);margin-bottom:3px">Nova equipe</div><strong style="color:${nCfg.c||'var(--pp)'}">${nCfg.sh}</strong>`
    : `<div style="color:var(--g300)">Selecione a equipe →</div>`;
  document.getElementById('mv-info').innerHTML = op
    ? `${op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')} · Total: <strong>${fR(op.rec)}</strong> · HO: <strong>${fR(op.ho)}</strong>`
    : '';
}

function mvApply(){
  const opName = document.getElementById('mv-op').value;
  const toEq   = document.getElementById('mv-eq').value;
  if(!opName || !toEq){ toast('⚠️ Selecione operador e equipe!'); return; }

  const op = ALL.find(o=>o.name===opName);
  if(!op){ toast('❌ Operador não encontrado!'); return; }
  if(op.eq === toEq){ toast('⚠️ Operador já está nesta equipe!'); return; }

  const fromEqObj = D.equipes.find(e=>e.name===op.eq);
  const toEqObj   = D.equipes.find(e=>e.name===toEq);
  if(!fromEqObj||!toEqObj){ toast('❌ Equipe não encontrada!'); return; }

  const fromCfg = EQ[op.eq]||{sh:op.eq};
  const toCfg   = EQ[toEq]||{sh:toEq};

  // Move in D
  fromEqObj.ops = fromEqObj.ops.filter(o=>o.name!==opName);
  op.eq = toEq;
  toEqObj.ops.push(op);
  toEqObj.ops.sort((a,b)=>b.rec-a.rec);

  // Recalc totals
  [fromEqObj, toEqObj].forEach(e=>{
    e.rec    = e.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.rec,0);
    e.ho     = e.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.ho,0);
    e.n_op   = e.ops.length;
    e.acordos= e.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.acordos,0);
  });

  // Remove empty equipes
  D.equipes = D.equipes.filter(e=>e.ops.length>0);

  // Persist move
  const ov = gGetOverrides();
  if(!ov.moves) ov.moves=[];
  ov.moves.push({op:opName, from:op.eq, to:toEq, ts:Date.now()});
  gSetOverrides(ov);
  fbPush('gestao', ov);

  rebuildAll();
  refreshAll();
  gestaoMoverInit();
  toast(`✅ ${opName.replace(/_/g,' ')} → ${toCfg.sh}!`);

  // Reset selects
  document.getElementById('mv-op').value='';
  document.getElementById('mv-eq').value='';
  document.getElementById('mv-preview').style.display='none';
}

function renderMvEqList(){
  document.getElementById('mv-eq-list').innerHTML = D.equipes.map(eq=>{
    const cfg = EQ[eq.name]||{c:'#888',bg:'#eee',ico:'📌',sh:eq.name};
    return `<div style="background:var(--g50);border:1px solid var(--g200);border-radius:var(--rl);padding:14px;border-left:4px solid ${cfg.c}">
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;margin-bottom:10px">
        <div style="font-size:18px">${cfg.ico}</div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:13px;color:var(--g900)">${cfg.sh}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500);font-weight:600">${eq.n_op} operadores</div>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-left:auto;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:16px;color:${cfg.c}">${fRK(eq.rec)}</div>
      </div>
      <div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:5px">
        ${eq.ops.map(op=>`
          <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;background:var(--w);
            border:1px solid var(--g200);border-radius:100px;padding:4px 10px;cursor:pointer;transition:all .2s"
            title="${fR(op.rec)}"
            onmouseover="this.style.borderColor='${cfg.c}';this.style.background='${cfg.c}12'"
            onmouseout="this.style.borderColor='var(--g200)';this.style.background='var(--w)'"
            onclick="document.getElementById('mv-op').value='${op.name}';mvPreview()">
            <div style="width:20px;height:20px;border-radius:5px;background:${cfg.c};
              display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:9px;color:#fff;font-weight:900">${ini(op.name)}</div>
            <span style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:var(--g700)">${op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')}</span>
          </div>`).join('')}
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

          <div style="width:${pct}%;height:100%;background:${cfg.c};border-radius:100px;transition:width 1s"></div>
        </div>
        <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500);margin-top:3px">${pct.toFixed(1)}% da meta</div></div>`:``}

      <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:5px;align-items:flex-end">
        <label style="font-size:9px;font-weight:700;color:var(--g500);letter-spacing:.8px;text-transform:uppercase">Meta Mensal (R$)</label>
        <input type="number" id="meta-eq-${eq.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_')}"

          onblur="this.style.boxShadow=''">
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function metasSave(){
  const metas = {};
  D.equipes.forEach(eq=>{
    const id  = 'meta-eq-'+eq.name.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g,'_');
    const inp = document.getElementById(id);
    const val = parseFloat(inp?.value||0);
    if(val>0) metas[eq.name] = val;
  });
  gSetMetas(metas);
  fbPush('metas_eq', metas);
  gestaoMetasInit();
  toast('✅ Metas salvas e sincronizadas para todos!');
}

// expose metas to other parts
function getMetaEquipe(eqName){ return gGetMetas()[eqName]||0; }

// ─────────────────────────────
// NOVO OPERADOR

function gestaoNovoInit(){
  // Populate equipe select
  const sel = document.getElementById('novo-eq');
  sel.innerHTML = '<option value="">— Selecione a equipe —</option>' +
    D.equipes.map(eq=>{
      const cfg=EQ[eq.name]||{sh:eq.name};
      return `<option value="${eq.name}">${cfg.ico||''} ${cfg.sh}</option>`;
    }).join('');

  renderNovoAdicionados();
}

function novoApply(){
  const nome = document.getElementById('novo-nome').value.trim().replace(/\s+/g,'_').toUpperCase();
  const eqNm = document.getElementById('novo-eq').value;
  const rec  = parseFloat(document.getElementById('novo-rec').value)||0;

  if(!nome){ toast('⚠️ Digite o nome do operador!'); return; }
  if(!eqNm){ toast('⚠️ Selecione a equipe!'); return; }
  if(ALL.find(o=>o.name===nome)){ toast('⚠️ Operador já existe: '+nome); return; }

  const ho = rec*0.25;
  const newOp = {
    name:nome, rec, ho, acordos:0, ligacoes:0,
    med_atraso:0, med_lig_baixa:0, daily:{}, tipos:{}, n_ag:0, val_ag:0, eq:eqNm
  };

  // Add to D
  const eqObj = D.equipes.find(e=>e.name===eqNm);
  if(!eqObj){ toast('❌ Equipe não encontrada!'); return; }
  eqObj.ops.push(newOp);
  eqObj.ops.sort((a,b)=>b.rec-a.rec);
  eqObj.rec   += rec;
  eqObj.ho    += ho;
  eqObj.n_op  = eqObj.ops.length;

  // Persist
  const ov = gGetOverrides();
  if(!ov.novos) ov.novos=[];
  ov.novos.push({name:nome, eq:eqNm, rec, ts:Date.now()});
  gSetOverrides(ov);
  fbPush('gestao', ov);

  rebuildAll();
  refreshAll();
  gestaoNovoInit();

  // Reset form
  document.getElementById('novo-nome').value='';
  document.getElementById('novo-rec').value='0';

  const cfg = EQ[eqNm]||{sh:eqNm};
  toast(`✅ ${nome.replace(/_/g,' ')} adicionado à ${cfg.sh}!`);
}

function renderNovoAdicionados(){
  const ov = gGetOverrides();
  const novos = ov.novos||[];
  const wrap = document.getElementById('novo-adicionados-wrap');
  const list = document.getElementById('novo-adicionados');
  if(!wrap||!list) return;
  if(novos.length===0){ wrap.style.display='none'; return; }
  wrap.style.display='block';
  list.innerHTML = novos.map((n,i)=>{
    const cfg=EQ[n.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:n.eq};
    const ts=new Date(n.ts).toLocaleString('pt-BR');
    return `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:9px 12px;
      background:var(--g50);border:1px solid var(--g200);border-radius:var(--rm);margin-bottom:6px">
      <div style="width:28px;height:28px;border-radius:7px;background:${cfg.c};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-weight:900;font-size:10px;color:#fff">${ini(n.name)}</div>
      <div style="flex:1">
        <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:12px;color:var(--g900)">${n.name.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div>
        <div style="font-size:10px;color:${cfg.c};font-weight:700">${cfg.sh}</div>
      </div>
      <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:15px;color:var(--pp)">${fR(n.rec)}</div>
      <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500)">${ts}</div>
      <button onclick="removeNovo(${i})"
        style="width:26px;height:26px;border-radius:6px;border:1px solid var(--g200);
        background:var(--w);color:var(--g500);cursor:pointer;font-size:12px;transition:all .2s"
        onmouseover="this.style.background='#FEF2F2';this.style.color='var(--danger)'"
        onmouseout="this.style.background='var(--w)';this.style.color='var(--g500)'">✕</button>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

function removeNovo(idx){
  const ov=gGetOverrides();
  if(!ov.novos||!ov.novos[idx]) return;
  const n=ov.novos[idx];
  // Remove from D
  const eqObj=D.equipes.find(e=>e.name===n.eq);
  if(eqObj){
    eqObj.ops=eqObj.ops.filter(o=>o.name!==n.name);
    eqObj.rec=eqObj.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.rec,0);
    eqObj.ho=eqObj.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.ho,0);
    eqObj.n_op=eqObj.ops.length;
  }
  ov.novos.splice(idx,1);
  gSetOverrides(ov);
  rebuildAll(); refreshAll(); renderNovoAdicionados();
  toast('↩ Operador removido!');
}

function gestaoSave(){
  metasSave();
  toast('💾 Tudo salvo com sucesso!');
}

// ── Load gestao overrides on start ──
function loadGestaoOverrides(){
  const ov=gGetOverrides();
  // Re-apply moves
  if(ov.moves && ov.moves.length>0){
    ov.moves.forEach(mv=>{
      const op=ALL.find(o=>o.name===mv.op);
      if(!op||op.eq===mv.to) return;
      const fromEq=D.equipes.find(e=>e.name===op.eq);
      const toEq=D.equipes.find(e=>e.name===mv.to);
      if(!fromEq||!toEq) return;
      fromEq.ops=fromEq.ops.filter(o=>o.name!==mv.op);
      op.eq=mv.to; toEq.ops.push(op); toEq.ops.sort((a,b)=>b.rec-a.rec);
      [fromEq,toEq].forEach(e=>{
        e.rec=e.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.rec,0);
        e.ho=e.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.ho,0);
        e.n_op=e.ops.length;
        e.acordos=e.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.acordos,0);
      });
    });
    D.equipes=D.equipes.filter(e=>e.ops.length>0);
    rebuildAll();
  }
  // Re-apply novos
  if(ov.novos && ov.novos.length>0){
    ov.novos.forEach(n=>{
      if(ALL.find(o=>o.name===n.name)) return;
      const eqObj=D.equipes.find(e=>e.name===n.eq);
      if(!eqObj) return;
      const ho=n.rec*0.25;
      const newOp={name:n.name,rec:n.rec,ho,acordos:0,ligacoes:0,
        med_atraso:0,med_lig_baixa:0,daily:{},tipos:{},n_ag:0,val_ag:0,eq:n.eq};
      eqObj.ops.push(newOp); eqObj.ops.sort((a,b)=>b.rec-a.rec);
      eqObj.rec+=n.rec; eqObj.ho+=ho; eqObj.n_op=eqObj.ops.length;
    });
    rebuildAll();
  }
}
