let importParsed = { found:[], missing:[] };


function impTab(tab){
  const isRec = tab==='rec';
  const tr = document.getElementById('imp-tab-rec');
  const ta = document.getElementById('imp-tab-ac');
  if(tr){ tr.style.color=isRec?'var(--pp)':'var(--g500)'; tr.style.background=isRec?'var(--ppl)':'var(--w)'; }
  if(ta){ ta.style.color=!isRec?'var(--info)':'var(--g500)'; ta.style.background=!isRec?'#EFF6FF':'var(--w)'; }
  document.querySelectorAll('.imp-view').forEach(v=>v.style.display='none');
  const el = document.getElementById('imp-'+tab);
  if(el) el.style.display='block';
}

function importInit(){
  // nothing to init — just clear status
  document.getElementById('import-status').textContent = '';
}

// ── PARSE raw TSV/CSV text ──
function importParse(raw){
  const lines = raw.trim().split(/\r?\n/);
  if(lines.length < 2) return null;

  // Detect separator: tab or semicolon or comma
  const firstLine = lines[0];
  const sep = firstLine.includes('\t') ? '\t'
    : firstLine.includes(';') ? ';' : ',';

  const headers = firstLine.split(sep).map(h=>h.trim().replace(/^"|"$/g,'').toLowerCase());

  // Find column indexes — flexible matching
  const colIdx = (candidates) => {
    for(const cand of candidates){
      const idx = headers.findIndex(h=>h.includes(cand));
      if(idx>=0) return idx;
    }
    return -1;
  };

  const iCob  = colIdx(['cobradora','operador','cobrador','nome']);
  const iRec  = colIdx(['recebido','rec ','valor rec','total rec']);
  const iHO   = colIdx(['total ho','ho','honorar']);
  const iEq   = colIdx(['equipe','subgrupo','time','squad']);

  if(iCob < 0 || iRec < 0){
    return {error: `Colunas não encontradas. Encontrado: ${headers.join(', ')}. Necessário: "Cobradora" e "Recebido".`};
  }

  // Accumulate per operator
  const acc = {}; // { opName: { ho, eq } }

  for(let i=1; i<lines.length; i++){
    const row = lines[i].split(sep).map(c=>c.trim().replace(/^"|"$/g,''));
    if(row.length <= iCob || row.length <= iRec) continue;
    const opName = row[iCob].trim();
    if(!opName) continue;
    const recVal = parseFloat(row[iRec].replace(',','.')) || 0;
    const hoVal  = iHO>=0 ? (parseFloat(row[iHO].replace(',','.')) || 0) : recVal;
    const eq     = iEq>=0 ? row[iEq].trim() : '';
    if(!acc[opName]) acc[opName] = { ho:0, eq };
    acc[opName].ho += recVal; // "Recebido" = HO
  }

  // Fuzzy match — Levenshtein distance simples
  function levenshtein(a, b){
    const m=a.length, n=b.length;
    const dp=Array.from({length:m+1},(_,i)=>Array.from({length:n+1},(_,j)=>i===0?j:j===0?i:0));
    for(let i=1;i<=m;i++) for(let j=1;j<=n;j++)
      dp[i][j]=a[i-1]===b[j-1]?dp[i-1][j-1]:1+Math.min(dp[i-1][j],dp[i][j-1],dp[i-1][j-1]);
    return dp[m][n];
  }
  function fuzzyMatch(name){
    const norm = s=>s.toLowerCase().replace(/[_\s.-]/g,'');
    const n = norm(name);
    let best=null, bestDist=Infinity;
    ALL.forEach(o=>{
      const d = levenshtein(n, norm(o.name));
      if(d<bestDist){ bestDist=d; best=o; }
    });
    return bestDist<=3 ? best : null; // tolerância de 3 chars
  }

  // Match against ALL operators
  const found   = [];
  const missing = [];

  Object.entries(acc).forEach(([name, data])=>{
    const totalReal = data.ho / 0.25;
    const normalize = s => s.toLowerCase().replace(/[_\s]/g,'');
    const matched = ALL.find(o => normalize(o.name) === normalize(name));

    if(matched){
      found.push({
        rawName:  name,
        opName:   matched.name,
        eq:       matched.eq,
        hoImport: data.ho,
        recImport:totalReal,
        recCurrent: matched.rec,
        hoCurrent:  matched.ho,
        diff: totalReal - matched.rec,
      });
    } else {
      const suggestion = fuzzyMatch(name);
      missing.push({ rawName:name, ho:data.ho, totalReal, eq:data.eq, suggestion });
    }
  });

  // Sort by totalReal desc
  found.sort((a,b)=>b.recImport-a.recImport);
  missing.sort((a,b)=>b.totalReal-a.totalReal);

  return { found, missing, sep, iCob, iRec, totalLines: lines.length-1 };
}

// ── PREVIEW (live as user types) ──
function importPreview(raw){
  if(!raw || raw.trim().length < 10){
    document.getElementById('import-preview-wrap').style.display='none';
    document.getElementById('import-status').textContent='';
    return;
  }
  const result = importParse(raw);
  if(!result || result.error){
    document.getElementById('import-status').textContent = result?.error || 'Formato não reconhecido';
    document.getElementById('import-status').style.color = 'var(--danger)';
    document.getElementById('import-preview-wrap').style.display='none';
    return;
  }

  importParsed = result;
  document.getElementById('import-status').textContent =
    result.totalLines+' linhas lidas · '+result.found.length+' operadores encontrados';
  document.getElementById('import-status').style.color = 'var(--ok)';

  // Summary
  document.getElementById('import-summary').textContent =
    result.found.length+' de '+(result.found.length+result.missing.length)+' operadores identificados';
  document.getElementById('ptab-ok-n').textContent  = result.found.length;
  document.getElementById('ptab-miss-n').textContent = result.missing.length;

  // Render preview OK
  const totalImport = result.found.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.recImport,0);
  const totalHoImport = totalImport*0.25;
  document.getElementById('import-preview-ok').innerHTML =
    // totals row
    `<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:36px 1fr 130px 130px 130px 110px;
      gap:10px;padding:10px 18px;background:var(--ppd);align-items:center">
      <span></span>
      <span style="font-weight:900;font-size:12px;color:#fff">TOTAL A IMPORTAR</span>
      <span style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:15px;color:#4ADE80;text-align:right">${fR(totalImport)}</span>
      <span style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:15px;color:#67E8F9;text-align:right">${fR(totalHoImport)}</span>
      <span></span><span></span>
    </div>` +
    // header
    `<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:36px 1fr 130px 130px 130px 110px;
      gap:10px;padding:8px 18px;background:var(--g50);border-bottom:1px solid var(--g200);
      font-size:10px;font-weight:800;color:var(--g500);letter-spacing:1px;text-transform:uppercase">
      <span></span><span>Operador</span>
      <span style="text-align:right">Total Importado</span>
      <span style="text-align:right">HO (25%)</span>
      <span style="text-align:right">Total Atual</span>
      <span style="text-align:right">Diferença</span>
    </div>` +
    result.found.map(r=>{
      const cfg = EQ[r.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:r.eq};
      const diffColor = r.diff>0 ? 'var(--ok)' : r.diff<0 ? 'var(--danger)' : 'var(--g500)';
      const diffSign  = r.diff>0 ? '+' : '';
      const changed   = Math.abs(r.diff) > 0.01;
      return `<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:36px 1fr 130px 130px 130px 110px;
        gap:10px;padding:9px 18px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--g100);align-items:center;
        background:${changed?'#F0FDF4':'var(--w)'}">
        <div style="width:28px;height:28px;border-radius:7px;background:${cfg.c};
          display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-weight:900;font-size:10px;color:#fff">
          ${ini(r.opName)}</div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:12px;color:var(--g900)">${r.opName.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:${cfg.c};font-weight:700">${cfg.sh}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:14px;color:var(--pp);text-align:right">${fR(r.recImport)}</div>
        <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:13px;color:var(--ok);text-align:right">${fR(r.hoImport)}</div>
        <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:13px;color:var(--g500);text-align:right">${fR(r.recCurrent)}</div>
        <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:14px;color:${diffColor};text-align:right;font-weight:800">
          ${changed ? diffSign+fR(r.diff) : '—'}
        </div>
      </div>`;
    }).join('');

  // Render missing — with fuzzy suggestions
  if(result.missing.length > 0){
    const normStr = s => s.toLowerCase().replace(/[_\s]/g,'');
    const levenshtein = (a,b) => {
      const m=a.length,n=b.length;
      const d=Array.from({length:m+1},(_,i)=>[i,...Array(n).fill(0)]);
      for(let j=0;j<=n;j++) d[0][j]=j;
      for(let i=1;i<=m;i++) for(let j=1;j<=n;j++)
        d[i][j]=a[i-1]===b[j-1]?d[i-1][j-1]:1+Math.min(d[i-1][j],d[i][j-1],d[i-1][j-1]);
      return d[m][n];
    };
    const getSugg = raw => {
      const nr=normStr(raw); let best=null,bd=99;
      ALL.forEach(op=>{ const dist=levenshtein(nr,normStr(op.name)); if(dist<bd&&dist<=4){bd=dist;best=op;} });
      return best;
    };
    document.getElementById('import-preview-miss').innerHTML =
      `<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--warn);font-weight:700;margin-bottom:10px;background:#FFFBEB;border:1px solid #FCD34D;border-radius:var(--rm);padding:9px 14px">
        ⚠️ Estes operadores não foram encontrados. Verifique a grafia ou adicione em <strong>Gestão → Novo Operador</strong>.
      </div>` +
      result.missing.map(m=>{
        const sugg=getSugg(m.rawName);
        return `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:9px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--g100)">
          <div style="width:28px;height:28px;border-radius:7px;background:var(--g200);
            display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:var(--g500);flex-shrink:0">?</div>
          <div style="flex:1;min-width:0">
            <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:12px;color:var(--g900)">${m.rawName}</div>
            <div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--g500);font-weight:600">${m.eq||'Equipe não identificada'}</div>
            ${sugg?`<div style="font-size:10px;margin-top:3px;color:#B45309;font-weight:700">💡 Possível correspondência: <span style="color:var(--g700);background:var(--g100);padding:1px 6px;border-radius:4px">${sugg.name.replace(/_/g,' ')}</span></div>`:''}
          </div>
          <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:14px;color:var(--warn);flex-shrink:0">${fR(m.totalReal)}</div>
        </div>`;}).join('');
  }

  document.getElementById('import-preview-wrap').style.display='block';
  importPTab('ok');
}

// ── TAB SWITCH in preview ──
function importPTab(tab){
  const isOk = tab==='ok';
  const tok  = document.getElementById('ptab-ok');
  const tmiss= document.getElementById('ptab-miss');
  const pok  = document.getElementById('import-preview-ok');
  const pmiss= document.getElementById('import-preview-miss');
  if(!tok||!tmiss||!pok||!pmiss) return;

  tok.style.color  = isOk ? 'var(--pp)' : 'var(--g500)';
  tok.style.borderBottomColor = isOk ? 'var(--pp)' : 'transparent';
  tok.style.background = isOk ? 'var(--ppl)' : 'transparent';

  tmiss.style.color = !isOk ? 'var(--warn)' : 'var(--g500)';
  tmiss.style.borderBottomColor = !isOk ? 'var(--warn)' : 'transparent';
  tmiss.style.background = !isOk ? '#FFFBEB' : 'transparent';

  pok.style.display  = isOk ? 'block' : 'none';
  pmiss.style.display= !isOk ? 'block' : 'none';
}

// ── APPLY IMPORT ──
function importApply(){
  if(!importParsed.found || importParsed.found.length===0){
    toast('⚠️ Nenhum dado para importar. Cole o relatório primeiro!');
    return;
  }

  let updated=0, unchanged=0;

  importParsed.found.forEach(r=>{
    const op = ALL.find(o=>o.name===r.opName);
    if(!op) return;
    if(Math.abs(r.recImport - op.rec) < 0.01){ unchanged++; return; }

    // Update in D
    op.rec = r.recImport;
    op.ho  = r.hoImport;

    // Update in equipe
    const eqObj = D.equipes.find(e=>e.name===op.eq);
    if(eqObj){
      eqObj.rec = eqObj.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.rec,0);
      eqObj.ho  = eqObj.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.ho,0);
    }
    updated++;
  });

  rebuildAll();
  refreshAll();

  // Save to localStorage as override
  const ov = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cofen_op_overrides')||'{}');
  importParsed.found.forEach(r=>{ ov[r.opName]=r.recImport; });
  localStorage.setItem('cofen_op_overrides', JSON.stringify(ov));

  const totalImportado = importParsed.found.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.recImport,0);
  toast(`✅ ${updated} operadores atualizados! Total: ${fRK(totalImportado)} · HO: ${fRK(totalImportado*0.25)}`);

  markImportDone('rec');

  // Update preview with green confirmation
  document.getElementById('import-status').textContent =
    `✅ Importação concluída! ${updated} atualizados, ${unchanged} sem alteração · Total: ${fRK(totalImportado)}`;
  document.getElementById('import-status').style.color='var(--ok)';

  // Refresh preview to show new diffs (all = 0 now)
  importPreview(document.getElementById('import-area').value);
}

function importClear(){
  document.getElementById('import-area').value='';
  document.getElementById('import-preview-wrap').style.display='none';
  document.getElementById('import-status').textContent='';
  importParsed={found:[],missing:[]};
}

function acordosInit(){
  acCalcKPIs();
  acRenderRanking();
  acRenderFechamento();
}

function acTab(view, el){
  document.querySelectorAll('.ac-stab').forEach(t=>{
    t.style.color='var(--g500)';
    t.style.borderBottomColor='transparent';
    t.style.background='transparent';
  });
  el.style.color='var(--pp)'; el.style.borderBottomColor='var(--pp)'; el.style.background='var(--ppl)';
  document.querySelectorAll('.acview').forEach(v=>v.style.display='none');
  document.getElementById('acv-'+view).style.display='block';
}

function acCalcKPIs(){
  const totG=ALL.reduce((s,o)=>s+(o.gerados||0),0);
  const totP=ALL.reduce((s,o)=>s+(o.pagos||0),0);
  const totAv=ALL.reduce((s,o)=>s+(o.avista||0),0);
  const totPend=ALL.reduce((s,o)=>s+(o.pendentes||0),0);
  const taxa=totG>0?(totP/totG*100).toFixed(1):0;
  const ticket=totP>0?(ALL.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.rec,0)/totP):0;
  const s=(id,v)=>{const e=document.getElementById(id);if(e)e.textContent=v};
  s('ac-total-gerados',totG.toLocaleString('pt-BR'));
  s('ac-total-pagos',totP.toLocaleString('pt-BR'));
  s('ac-taxa',taxa+'%');
  s('ac-avista',totAv.toLocaleString('pt-BR'));
  s('ac-pend',totPend.toLocaleString('pt-BR'));
  s('ac-ticket',fRK(ticket));
}

function acRenderRanking(){
  // Sort by acordos pagos desc
  const sorted=[...ALL].sort((a,b)=>(b.pagos||0)-(a.pagos||0));
  const maxG=sorted[0]?.gerados||1;
  document.getElementById('ac-ranking-list').innerHTML=sorted.map((op,i)=>{
    const cfg=EQ[op.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:op.eq};
    const r=i+1;
    const g=op.gerados||0, p=op.pagos||0, av=op.avista||0, m3=op.mais3dias||0;
    const taxa=g>0?(p/g*100).toFixed(1):'100';
    const avPct=p>0?(av/p*100).toFixed(0):'0';
    const tk=op.ticket||0;
    const taxaColor=parseFloat(taxa)>=40?'var(--ok)':parseFloat(taxa)>=20?'var(--warn)':'var(--danger)';
    const cls=r===1?'r1':r===2?'r2':r===3?'r3':'';
    return `<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:42px 1fr 80px 80px 80px 80px 80px 90px;
      gap:10px;align-items:center;padding:10px 16px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--g100);
      cursor:pointer;transition:background .2s;background:${r<=3?'rgba(0,168,107,.03)':'var(--w)'}"
      onclick="openM('${op.name}')"
      onmouseover="this.style.background='var(--g50)'"
      onmouseout="this.style.background='${r<=3?'rgba(0,168,107,.03)':'var(--w)'}'"
      >
      <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:18px;color:${r===1?'var(--pp)':r===2?'var(--g300)':r===3?'#CD7F32':'var(--g300)'};text-align:center">
        ${r<=3?['🥇','🥈','🥉'][r-1]:r+'°'}
      </div>
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;min-width:0">
        <div style="width:28px;height:28px;border-radius:7px;background:${cfg.c};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-weight:900;font-size:10px;color:#fff;flex-shrink:0">${ini(op.name)}</div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:12px;color:var(--g900);white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">${op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:${cfg.c};font-weight:700">${cfg.sh}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:center;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:18px;color:var(--info)">${g}</div>
      <div style="text-align:center;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:18px;color:var(--ok)">${p}</div>
      <div style="text-align:center">
        <div style="font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:16px;color:${taxaColor}">${taxa}%</div>
        <div style="background:var(--g100);border-radius:100px;height:3px;overflow:hidden;margin-top:2px">
          <div style="width:${taxa}%;height:100%;background:${taxaColor};border-radius:100px"></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:center;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:16px;color:var(--ok)">${av} <span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--g500)">(${avPct}%)</span></div>
      <div style="text-align:center;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:16px;color:${m3>g*0.3?'var(--danger)':'var(--g500)'}">${m3}</div>
      <div style="text-align:right;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:15px;color:var(--pp)">${fR(tk)}</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

    const cfg=EQ[op.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:op.eq};

    const tk=op.ticket||0;
    const taxa=g>0?(p/g*100):100;

      gap:10px;align-items:center;padding:9px 14px;
      border-radius:var(--rm);margin-bottom:4px;cursor:pointer;transition:all .2s;

      onclick="openM('${op.name}')"

      >
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">

        <div>
          <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:12px;color:var(--g900)">${op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:${cfg.c};font-weight:700">${cfg.sh}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:center;font-weight:800;font-size:14px;color:var(--info)">${g}</div>
      <div style="text-align:center">
        <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:14px;color:var(--ok)">${p}</div>
        <div style="font-size:9px;color:${taxaColor};font-weight:700">${taxa.toFixed(0)}%</div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:center;font-weight:700;font-size:13px;color:var(--ok)">${av}</div>
      <div style="text-align:center;font-weight:700;font-size:13px;color:${m3>g*0.3?'var(--danger)':'var(--g500)'}">${m3}</div>
      <div style="text-align:right;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:14px;color:var(--pp)">${fR(tk)}</div>
      <div style="text-align:right;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:14px;color:var(--pp)">${fR(op.rec)}</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

// ── IMPORT ACORDOS ──
let acImportParsed=[];

function acImportPreview(raw){
  if(!raw||raw.trim().length<5){
    document.getElementById('ac-import-preview').style.display='none';
    document.getElementById('ac-import-status').textContent='';
    return;
  }
  const lines=raw.trim().split(/\r?\n/);
  if(lines.length<2) return;
  const sep=lines[0].includes('\t')?'\t':lines[0].includes(';')?';':',';
  const headers=lines[0].split(sep).map(h=>h.trim().replace(/^"|"$/g,'').toLowerCase()
    .replace('usuário','usuario').replace('dt.','dt'));

  // flexible column detection
  const idx=candidates=>{ for(const cand of candidates){ const i=headers.findIndex(h=>h.includes(cand)); if(i>=0) return i; } return -1; };
  const iCob  = idx(['usuario','cobrador','operador','nome']);
  const iDtPg = idx(['dtpagamento','dt pagamento','pagamento','baixa']);
  const iDtPv = idx(['dtprev','dt prev','prev.pgto','agendamento','prev pgto']);

  if(iCob<0){ document.getElementById('ac-import-status').textContent='⚠️ Coluna "Usuário" não encontrada'; return; }

  const normalize=s=>s.toLowerCase().replace(/[_\s]/g,'');
  const acc={};
  for(let i=1;i<lines.length;i++){
    const row=lines[i].split(sep).map(v=>v.trim().replace(/^"|"$/g,''));
    if(row.length<=iCob) continue;
    const nm=row[iCob]||''; if(!nm||nm==='nan'||nm==='-') continue;
    if(!acc[nm]) acc[nm]={g:0,p:0,ag:0};
    acc[nm].g++;
    const pgVal = iDtPg>=0 ? row[iDtPg]||'' : '';
    const pvVal = iDtPv>=0 ? row[iDtPv]||'' : '';
    const isPago = pgVal&&pgVal!==''&&pgVal.toLowerCase()!=='nat'&&pgVal.toLowerCase()!=='nan'&&pgVal!=='NaT';
    if(isPago) acc[nm].p++;
    else if(pvVal&&pvVal!==''&&pvVal.toLowerCase()!=='nat'&&pvVal.toLowerCase()!=='nan') acc[nm].ag++;
  }

  acImportParsed=Object.entries(acc).map(([nm,d])=>{
    const matched=ALL.find(o=>normalize(o.name)===normalize(nm));
    return {rawName:nm,opName:matched?.name||null,g:d.g,p:d.p,ag:d.ag,matched:!!matched};
  });
  const found=acImportParsed.filter(r=>r.matched);
  const missing=acImportParsed.filter(r=>!r.matched);

  document.getElementById('ac-import-status').textContent=
    found.length+' operadores encontrados · '+missing.length+' não reconhecidos · '+(lines.length-1)+' linhas';
  document.getElementById('ac-import-status').style.color = found.length>0?'var(--ok)':'var(--danger)';
  document.getElementById('ac-import-summary').textContent=
    'Total: '+found.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.g,0)+' gerados, '+found.reduce((s,r)=>s+r.p,0)+' pagos';

  // Build found list
  let listHTML = found.map(r=>{
    const op=ALL.find(o=>o.name===r.opName);
    const cfg=EQ[op?.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:''};
    const ef=r.g>0?(r.p/r.g*100).toFixed(1):'0';
    const efCol=parseFloat(ef)>=40?'var(--ok)':parseFloat(ef)>=20?'var(--warn)':'var(--danger)';
    return `<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 70px 70px 70px 75px;gap:10px;
      padding:9px 16px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--g100);align-items:center;
      background:${r.p>0?'#F0FDF4':'var(--w)'}">
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">
        <div style="width:26px;height:26px;border-radius:7px;background:${cfg.c};
          display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:9px;font-weight:900;color:#fff">${ini(r.opName)}</div>
        <div>
          <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:12px;color:var(--g900)">${r.opName.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;color:${cfg.c};font-weight:700">${cfg.sh}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div style="text-align:center;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:18px;color:var(--info)">${r.g}</div>
      <div style="text-align:center;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:18px;color:var(--ok)">${r.p}</div>
      <div style="text-align:center;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:16px;color:var(--warn)">${r.ag}</div>
      <div style="text-align:center;font-family:Bebas Neue,sans-serif;font-size:16px;color:${efCol}">${ef}%</div>
    </div>`;
  }).join('');

  // Append missing with suggestions
  if(missing.length>0){
    listHTML += `<div style="padding:10px 16px;background:#FFFBEB;border-top:2px solid #FCD34D">
      <div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:800;color:#92400E;margin-bottom:8px">⚠️ ${missing.length} operadores não encontrados:</div>
      ${missing.map(m=>{
        const sugg = acImportParsed.find(x=>!x.matched&&x.rawName===m.rawName)?.suggestion||null;
        return `<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;padding:5px 0;border-bottom:1px solid #FDE68A">
          <div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:800;color:var(--g900);flex:1">${m.rawName}</div>
          ${sugg?`<div style="font-size:10px;color:#B45309;font-weight:700">💡 Talvez: ${sugg.name.replace(/_/g,' ')}</div>`:''}
          <div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:800;color:var(--warn)">${m.g} acordos</div>
        </div>`;
      }).join('')}
    </div>`;
  }

  document.getElementById('ac-import-list').innerHTML = listHTML;

  acImportParsed=found; // only keep matched
  document.getElementById('ac-import-preview').style.display='block';
}

function acImportApply(){
  if(!acImportParsed.length){toast('⚠️ Nenhum dado para importar!');return;}
  acImportParsed.forEach(r=>{
    const op=ALL.find(o=>o.name===r.opName);
    if(!op) return;
    op.gerados    = r.g;
    op['pagos']   = r.p;
    op['pendentes']= r.g - r.p;
    op['agendados']= r.ag || (r.g - r.p);
    op['eficiencia']= r.g>0 ? parseFloat((r.p/r.g*100).toFixed(1)) : 0;
    if(r.p>0) op['ticket'] = parseFloat((op.rec/r.p).toFixed(2));
  });
  acordosInit();
  markImportDone('ac');
  toast('✅ Acordos atualizados para '+acImportParsed.length+' operadores!');
}



// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// FOTOS DOS OPERADORES
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
let currentModalOp = null;

function photoGetAll(){ try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cofen_photos')||'{}')}catch(e){return {}} }
function photoSet(opName, url){
  const all = photoGetAll();
  if(url) all[opName] = url; else delete all[opName];
  localStorage.setItem('cofen_photos', JSON.stringify(all));
  // Sync to shared storage if available
  if(window.storage){ window.storage.set('photos', JSON.stringify(all), true).catch(()=>{}); }
}
function photoGet(opName){ return photoGetAll()[opName] || null; }

function photoUpload(){
  document.getElementById('m-photo-file').click();
}

function photoFileSelected(inp){
  if(!inp.files||!inp.files[0]) return;
  const file = inp.files[0];
  const reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = e => {
    const url = e.target.result;
    if(currentModalOp){
      photoSet(currentModalOp, url);
      renderModalPhoto(currentModalOp, EQ[ALL.find(o=>o.name===currentModalOp)?.eq]||{c:'#888'});
      toast('✅ Foto salva para ' + currentModalOp.replace(/_/g,' ') + '!');
    }
  };
  reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  inp.value='';
}


// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// GRÁFICO EVOLUÇÃO SEMANAL — MODAL
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
function renderWeeklyChart(op){
  destroyC('m-weekly');
  const canvas = document.getElementById('m-weekly-chart');
  if(!canvas) return;
  const cfg = EQ[op.eq]||{c:'#888'};

  // Group daily values into weeks (Mon–Fri buckets)
  // Week 1: days 1-5, Week 2: 6-10, Week 3: 11-15, Week 4: 16-20, Week 5: 21+
  const weeks = ['Sem 1\n(1–5)', 'Sem 2\n(6–10)', 'Sem 3\n(11–15)', 'Sem 4\n(16–20)', 'Sem 5\n(21+)'];
  const weekTotals = [0,0,0,0,0];
  Object.entries(op.daily||{}).forEach(([d,v])=>{
    const day = parseInt(d);
    if(day<=5)       weekTotals[0]+=v;
    else if(day<=10) weekTotals[1]+=v;
    else if(day<=15) weekTotals[2]+=v;
    else if(day<=20) weekTotals[3]+=v;
    else             weekTotals[4]+=v;
  });

  // Meta semanal esperada (meta_ind / 4.33 semanas)
  const metaInd = getMetaOp(op.name);
  const metaSem = metaInd > 0 ? metaInd / 4.33 : 0;

  // Colors per bar based on projection
  const barColors = weekTotals.map(v => {
    if(!metaSem) return cfg.c+'CC';
    const pct = v/metaSem*100;
    if(pct>=100) return 'rgba(0,168,107,0.85)';
    if(pct>=80)  return 'rgba(59,130,246,0.85)';
    if(pct>=50)  return 'rgba(245,158,11,0.85)';
    return v===0 ? 'rgba(200,200,200,0.4)' : 'rgba(239,68,68,0.8)';
  });

  charts['m-weekly'] = new Chart(canvas.getContext('2d'),{
    type:'bar',
    data:{
      labels:['S1 (1-5)','S2 (6-10)','S3 (11-15)','S4 (16-20)','S5 (21+)'],
      datasets:[
        {
          label:'Recebido',
          data: weekTotals,
          backgroundColor: barColors,
          borderRadius:5,
          borderSkipped:false
        },
        ...(metaSem>0 ? [{
          label:'Meta/Semana',
          data: Array(5).fill(metaSem),
          type:'line',
          borderColor: cfg.c,
          borderWidth:1.5,
          borderDash:[4,3],
          pointRadius:0,
          fill:false,
          tension:0
        }] : [])
      ]
    },
    options:{
      responsive:true,
      maintainAspectRatio:false,
      plugins:{
        legend:{display:false},
        tooltip:{callbacks:{
          label: ctx => 'R$ '+ctx.raw.toLocaleString('pt-BR',{minimumFractionDigits:0}),
          afterLabel: ctx => {
            if(ctx.datasetIndex>0) return '';
            if(!metaSem) return '';
            const pct = (ctx.raw/metaSem*100).toFixed(0);
            const status = pct>=100?'✅ Meta':pct>=80?'🔵 80%+':pct>=50?'⚠️ 50%+':'🔴 Baixo';
            return status+' ('+pct+'% da meta sem.)';
          }
        }}
      },
      scales:{
        x:{grid:{display:false},ticks:{font:{size:9},color:'#7A8899'}},
        y:{grid:{color:'rgba(0,0,0,.05)'},ticks:{font:{size:9},color:'#7A8899',callback:v=>'R$'+v/1000+'K'}}
      }
    }
  });
}

function renderModalPhoto(opName, cfg){
  const photo = photoGet(opName);
  const wrap  = document.getElementById('m-photo-wrap');
  const btn   = document.getElementById('m-photo-btn');
  if(!wrap) return;
  if(photo){
    wrap.innerHTML = `<div style="position:relative">
      <img src="${photo}" class="op-photo" alt="${opName}">
      <button onclick="photoRemove('${opName}')"
        style="position:absolute;top:-6px;right:-6px;width:20px;height:20px;border-radius:50%;
        border:none;background:var(--danger);color:#fff;cursor:pointer;font-size:10px;
        display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center">✕</button>
    </div>`;
    if(btn) btn.textContent='📷 Trocar foto';
  } else {
    wrap.innerHTML = `<div class="op-photo-placeholder" style="background:${cfg.c}">${ini(opName)}</div>`;
    if(btn) btn.textContent='📷 Adicionar foto';
  }
}

function photoRemove(opName){
  photoSet(opName, null);
  const cfg = EQ[ALL.find(o=>o.name===opName)?.eq]||{c:'#888'};
  renderModalPhoto(opName, cfg);
  toast('🗑 Foto removida');
}

// Load photos from shared storage on init
async function loadSharedPhotos(){
  if(!window.storage) return;
  try {
    const res = await window.storage.get('photos', true);
    if(res && res.value){
      const remote = JSON.parse(res.value);
      const local  = photoGetAll();
      const merged = {...local, ...remote};
      localStorage.setItem('cofen_photos', JSON.stringify(merged));
    }
  } catch(e){}
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// SHARED REAL-TIME SYNC via localStorage broadcast
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// Uses BroadcastChannel for same-origin multi-tab sync
let syncChannel = null;
try {
  syncChannel = new BroadcastChannel('cofen_sync');
  syncChannel.onmessage = e => {
    if(e.data.type === 'rec_update'){
      // Another tab updated operator values — reload overrides and refresh
      const ov = JSON.parse(e.data.payload||'{}');
      Object.keys(ov).forEach(nm=>{
        const op=ALL.find(o=>o.name===nm);
        if(!op) return;
        op.rec=ov[nm]; op.ho=op.rec*0.25;
      });
      // Recalc equipes
      D.equipes.forEach(eq=>{
        eq.rec=eq.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.rec,0);
        eq.ho =eq.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.ho,0);
      });
      rebuildAll();
      refreshAll();
    }
    if(e.data.type === 'rd_update'){
      // Recebimento do dia update from another tab
      if(document.getElementById('pg-recdia')?.classList.contains('on')) rdRender();
    }
    if(e.data.type === 'photo_update'){
      const photos = JSON.parse(e.data.payload||'{}');
      localStorage.setItem('cofen_photos', JSON.stringify(photos));
    }
    if(e.data.type === 'meta_update'){
      // Outra aba editou total/meta — aplicar aqui também
      const d = JSON.parse(e.data.payload||'{}');
      const remTotal = parseFloat(d.total)||0;
      const remMeta  = parseFloat(d.meta)||META_DEFAULT;
      if(remTotal > 0) overrideTotalRec = remTotal;
      meta = remMeta;
      localStorage.setItem('cofen_total', remTotal);
      localStorage.setItem('cofen_meta',  remMeta);
      const inpTotal = document.getElementById('inp-total');
      const inpMeta  = document.getElementById('inp-meta');
      if(inpTotal && remTotal > 0) inpTotal.value = remTotal;
      if(inpMeta) inpMeta.value = remMeta;
      refreshAll();
    }
  };
} catch(e){}

function syncBroadcast(type, payload){
  try{ if(syncChannel) syncChannel.postMessage({type, payload}); }catch(e){}
}

// Patch rdSetSaved to broadcast
const _rdSetSaved_orig = rdSetSaved;
function rdSetSaved(map){
  _rdSetSaved_orig(map);
  syncBroadcast('rd_update', JSON.stringify(map));
}

// Patch photoSet to broadcast
const _photoSet_orig = photoSet;
function photoSet(opName, url){
  _photoSet_orig(opName, url);
  syncBroadcast('photo_update', JSON.stringify(photoGetAll()));
}

// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// MODO TV
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
let tvIdx=0, tvTimer=null, tvPaused=false, tvList=[];
const TV_INTERVAL = 8000; // 8s per operator

function tvStart(){
  // Build list sorted by total real desc
  tvList = [...ALL].sort((a,b)=>b.rec-a.rec);
  tvIdx  = 0;
  tvPaused = false;
  document.getElementById('tv-overlay').classList.add('on');
  document.getElementById('tv-pause-btn').textContent='⏸ Pausar';
  tvBuildDots();
  tvShow(0);
  tvSchedule();
}

function tvStop(){
  clearTimeout(tvTimer);
  document.getElementById('tv-overlay').classList.remove('on');
}

function tvSchedule(){
  clearTimeout(tvTimer);
  if(!tvPaused) tvTimer = setTimeout(()=>{ tvNext(); }, TV_INTERVAL);
}

function tvTogglePause(){
  tvPaused=!tvPaused;
  document.getElementById('tv-pause-btn').textContent=tvPaused?'▶ Retomar':'⏸ Pausar';
  if(!tvPaused) tvSchedule();
  else clearTimeout(tvTimer);
}

function tvNext(){
  tvIdx=(tvIdx+1)%tvList.length;
  tvShow(tvIdx);
  tvSchedule();
}

function tvPrev(){
  tvIdx=(tvIdx-1+tvList.length)%tvList.length;
  tvShow(tvIdx);
  tvSchedule();
}

function tvBuildDots(){
  const max=Math.min(tvList.length,20);
  document.getElementById('tv-dots').innerHTML=
    Array.from({length:max},(_,i)=>`<div class="tv-dot${i===0?' on':''}" onclick="tvGoTo(${i})"></div>`).join('');
}

function tvGoTo(i){ tvIdx=i; tvShow(i); tvSchedule(); }

function tvUpdateDots(){
  const dots=document.querySelectorAll('.tv-dot');
  dots.forEach((d,i)=>d.classList.toggle('on',i===tvIdx%dots.length));
}

function tvShow(idx){
  const op  = tvList[idx];
  const cfg = EQ[op.eq]||{c:'#888',bg:'#1a2330',ico:'⭐',sh:op.eq};
  const photo = photoGet(op.name);

  // Clock
  const now=new Date();
  document.getElementById('tv-clock-display').textContent=
    [now.getHours(),now.getMinutes(),now.getSeconds()].map(n=>String(n).padStart(2,'0')).join(':');

  // Acordos/eficiência
  const gerados  = op.gerados   || 0;
  const pagos    = op.pagos     || 0;
  const pendentes= op.pendentes || 0;
  const efPct    = gerados>0?(pagos/gerados*100).toFixed(1):'0';
  const efColor  = parseFloat(efPct)>=40?'#4ADE80':parseFloat(efPct)>=20?'#FCD34D':'#FCA5A5';

  // Agendamentos futuros próximos
  const agFuturo = op.ag_futuro||{};
  const agDates  = Object.entries(agFuturo).sort((a,b)=>a[0].localeCompare(b[0])).slice(0,4);
  const agTotal  = Object.values(agFuturo).reduce((s,v)=>s+v,0);

  // Tier
  const tier = op.rec>=20000?'⭐ S-TIER':op.rec>=10000?'A ALTA':op.rec>=5000?'B BOA':'C DEV';
  const tierColor = op.rec>=20000?'#4ADE80':op.rec>=10000?'#67E8F9':op.rec>=5000?'#FCD34D':'#FCA5A5';

  // Photo or avatar
  const photoHtml = photo
    ? `<img src="${photo}" class="tv-photo" alt="${op.name}">`
    : `<div class="tv-photo-placeholder" style="background:${cfg.c}">${ini(op.name)}</div>`;

  document.getElementById('tv-card').innerHTML=`
    <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:28px;margin-bottom:24px">
      ${photoHtml}
      <div style="flex:1;min-width:0">
        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;margin-bottom:4px">
          <div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:${tierColor};background:${tierColor}18;
            border:1px solid ${tierColor}33;padding:3px 10px;border-radius:100px;letter-spacing:1px">${tier}</div>
          <div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3);letter-spacing:2px;text-transform:uppercase">${idx+1} de ${tvList.length}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="tv-name">${op.name.replace(/_/g,' ').toUpperCase()}</div>
        <div class="tv-eq">${cfg.ico} ${cfg.sh}</div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr);gap:12px;margin-bottom:20px">
      <div class="tv-kpi" style="border-color:rgba(74,222,128,.2)">
        <div class="tv-kpi-l">Total Real</div>
        <div class="tv-kpi-v" style="color:#4ADE80">${fR(op.rec)}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="tv-kpi" style="border-color:rgba(103,232,249,.2)">
        <div class="tv-kpi-l">HO (25%)</div>
        <div class="tv-kpi-v" style="color:#67E8F9">${fR(op.ho)}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="tv-kpi">
        <div class="tv-kpi-l">Acordos Gerados</div>
        <div class="tv-kpi-v" style="color:#fff">${gerados}</div>
      </div>
      <div class="tv-kpi" style="border-color:${efColor}33">
        <div class="tv-kpi-l">Eficiência</div>
        <div class="tv-kpi-v" style="color:${efColor}">${efPct}%</div>
        <div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3);margin-top:3px">${pagos} pagos / ${pendentes} pend.</div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:16px">
      <div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.04);border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.08);border-radius:12px;padding:14px">
        <div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:rgba(255,255,255,.35);letter-spacing:1.5px;text-transform:uppercase;margin-bottom:10px">📅 Agendamentos Futuros (${agTotal})</div>
        ${agDates.length>0
          ? agDates.map(([dt,n])=>`<div class="tv-ag-row">
              <span style="color:rgba(255,255,255,.7)">${new Date(dt+'T12:00:00').toLocaleDateString('pt-BR',{weekday:'short',day:'2-digit',month:'2-digit'})}</span>
              <span style="color:#67E8F9;font-weight:800">${n} acordo${n>1?'s':''}</span>
            </div>`).join('')
          : '<div style="font-size:13px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.25);font-style:italic">Sem agendamentos futuros</div>'}
      </div>
      <div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.04);border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.08);border-radius:12px;padding:14px">
        <div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:rgba(255,255,255,.35);letter-spacing:1.5px;text-transform:uppercase;margin-bottom:10px">💳 Formas de Pagamento</div>
        ${Object.entries(op.tipos||{}).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]).slice(0,3).map(([k,v])=>{
          const tColors={"PIX":"#4ADE80","CARTÃO DE CRÉDITO":"#67E8F9","BOLETO NEGOCIAÇÃO":"#FCD34D"};
          const total=Object.values(op.tipos||{}).reduce((s,vv)=>s+vv,0);
          const pct=total>0?Math.round(v/total*100):0;
          return `<div class="tv-ag-row">
            <span style="color:rgba(255,255,255,.7);font-size:12px">${k.replace('NEGOCIAÇÃO','').trim()}</span>
            <span style="color:${tColors[k]||'#fff'};font-weight:800">${pct}%</span>
          </div>`;
        }).join('')}
      </div>
    </div>`;

  tvUpdateDots();

  // Reset + animate progress bar
  const bar = document.getElementById('tv-bar');
  bar.style.transition='none';
  bar.style.width='0%';
  bar.style.background=cfg.c||'var(--pp)';
  setTimeout(()=>{ bar.style.transition=`width ${TV_INTERVAL}ms linear`; bar.style.width='100%'; },50);
}

// Keyboard controls for TV
document.addEventListener('keydown', e=>{
  if(!document.getElementById('tv-overlay').classList.contains('on')) return;
  if(e.key==='Escape') tvStop();
  if(e.key==='ArrowRight'||e.key==='ArrowDown') tvNext();
  if(e.key==='ArrowLeft'||e.key==='ArrowUp') tvPrev();
  if(e.key===' '){ e.preventDefault(); tvTogglePause(); }
});

// Update TV clock every second
setInterval(()=>{
  if(document.getElementById('tv-overlay').classList.contains('on')){
    const now=new Date();
    const el=document.getElementById('tv-clock-display');
    if(el) el.textContent=[now.getHours(),now.getMinutes(),now.getSeconds()].map(n=>String(n).padStart(2,'0')).join(':');
  }
},1000);



function pulseSyncDot(){
  const dot=document.getElementById('sync-dot');
  if(!dot) return;
  dot.style.background='#FCD34D';
  dot.style.transform='scale(1.8)';
  setTimeout(()=>{dot.style.background='#4ADE80';dot.style.transform='scale(1)';},800);
}
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// FIREBASE SYNC — TEMPO REAL MULTI-DISPOSITIVO
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
let fbApp = null, fbDb = null, fbRoom = null;
let fbListeners = {};

function fbKey(){ return 'cofen_fb_cfg'; }
function fbLoadCfg(){ try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(fbKey())||'{}')}catch(e){return {}} }
function fbSaveCfg(cfg){ localStorage.setItem(fbKey(), JSON.stringify(cfg)); }

// ── MODAL CONTROLS ──
function syncModalOpen(){
  const cfg = fbLoadCfg();
  if(cfg.room) document.getElementById('sync-room').value = cfg.room;
  if(cfg.url)  { document.getElementById('sync-fburl').value = cfg.url; document.getElementById('sync-fb-field').style.display='block'; }
  document.getElementById('sync-modal').classList.add('on');
  syncUpdateStatus();
}
function syncModalClose(){ document.getElementById('sync-modal').classList.remove('on'); }
function syncRoomChanged(){
  document.getElementById('sync-fb-field').style.display='block';
}

// ── CONNECT ──
async function syncConnect(){
  const room = document.getElementById('sync-room').value.trim().replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/g,'-');
  const url  = document.getElementById('sync-fburl').value.trim().replace(/\/$/,'');
  if(!room){ toast('cofen-principal'); return; }
  if(!url||!url.startsWith('https')){ toast('https://cofen-dashboard-622a8-default-rtdb.firebaseio.com'); return; }

  syncSetStatus('connecting','🔄 Conectando...');
  document.getElementById('sync-connect-btn').textContent='⏳ Conectando...';
  document.getElementById('sync-connect-btn').disabled=true;

  try {
    // Init Firebase (or reuse)
    if(!fbApp){
      fbApp = firebase.initializeApp({
        databaseURL: url
      }, 'cofen-sync-'+Date.now());
    }
    fbDb   = firebase.database(fbApp);
    fbRoom = room;
    fbSaveCfg({room, url});

    // Test connection — REST ping first (works from local file)
    let connected = false;
    try {
      const restTest = await fetch(url+'/.json?shallow=true', {signal: AbortSignal.timeout(6000)});
      connected = restTest.ok || restTest.status === 200 || restTest.status === 204;
    } catch(e){ connected = false; }

    if(!connected){
      // fallback SDK check with longer timeout
      const testRef = fbDb.ref('.info/connected');
      await new Promise((resolve)=>{
        const timeout = setTimeout(()=>resolve(), 6000);
        testRef.on('value', snap=>{ if(snap.val()===true){ clearTimeout(timeout); resolve(); } });
      });
    }

    syncSetStatus('online','✅ Conectado em tempo real');
    document.getElementById('sync-connect-btn').textContent='✔ Conectado';
    document.getElementById('sync-connect-btn').disabled=false;
    document.getElementById('sync-topbtn').style.background='var(--ppl)';
    document.getElementById('sync-topbtn').style.color='var(--pp)';
    document.getElementById('sync-topbtn').textContent='🟢 Sync';
    toast('✅ Sync ativado! Sala: '+room);

    fbStartListening();
    fbSyncModalClose_auto();
  } catch(err){
    syncSetStatus('error','❌ Erro: '+err.message);
    document.getElementById('sync-connect-btn').textContent='🔗 Tentar novamente';
    document.getElementById('sync-connect-btn').disabled=false;
    toast('❌ Falha na conexão: '+err.message);
  }
}

function fbSyncModalClose_auto(){
  setTimeout(()=>syncModalClose(),1200);
}

function syncDisconnect(){
  if(fbListeners.rd)        { fbDb?.ref(fbRoom+'/rd').off(); }
  if(fbListeners.overrides) { fbDb?.ref(fbRoom+'/overrides').off(); }
  if(fbListeners.photos)    { fbDb?.ref(fbRoom+'/photos').off(); }
  if(fbListeners.meta)      { fbDb?.ref(fbRoom+'/meta').off(); }
  if(fbListeners.metas_eq)  { fbDb?.ref(fbRoom+'/metas_eq').off(); }
  if(fbListeners.metas_op)  { fbDb?.ref(fbRoom+'/metas_op').off(); }
  if(fbListeners.gestao)    { fbDb?.ref(fbRoom+'/gestao').off(); }
  fbListeners={};
  fbApp=null; fbDb=null; fbRoom=null;
  fbSaveCfg({});
  syncSetStatus('offline','⚫ Desconectado');
  document.getElementById('sync-topbtn').style.background='var(--w)';
  document.getElementById('sync-topbtn').textContent='🔗 Sync';
  toast('🔌 Sync desativado');
}

function syncSetStatus(state, msg){
  const dot  = document.getElementById('sync-status-dot');
  const text = document.getElementById('sync-status-text');
  if(!dot||!text) return;
  const colors = {online:'#4ADE80',connecting:'#FCD34D',error:'#EF4444',offline:'#94a3b8'};
  dot.style.background  = colors[state]||'#94a3b8';
  text.textContent = msg;
}
function syncUpdateStatus(){
  if(fbDb && fbRoom) syncSetStatus('online','✅ Conectado — Sala: '+fbRoom);
  else syncSetStatus('offline','⚫ Não conectado');
}

// ── FIREBASE LISTENERS ──
function fbStartListening(){
  if(!fbDb||!fbRoom) return;

  // ── Recebimento do dia (rd) ──
  fbDb.ref(fbRoom+'/rd').on('value', snap=>{
    const remote = snap.val();
    if(!remote) return;
    // Merge with local — remote wins per key
    const local = rdGetSaved();
    const merged = {...local, ...remote};
    // Only update if different from what we have
    const localStr = JSON.stringify(local);
    if(JSON.stringify(remote)!==localStr){
      localStorage.setItem(rdTodayKey(), JSON.stringify(merged));
      if(document.getElementById('pg-recdia')?.classList.contains('on')) rdRender();
      pulseSyncDot();
    }
  });
  fbListeners.rd = true;

  // ── Overrides (recebimento base) ──
  fbDb.ref(fbRoom+'/overrides').on('value', snap=>{
    const remote = snap.val();
    if(!remote) return;
    const local = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cofen_op_overrides')||'{}');
    if(JSON.stringify(remote)===JSON.stringify(local)) return;
    // Apply remote
    Object.entries(remote).forEach(([nm,val])=>{
      const op=ALL.find(o=>o.name===nm);
      if(!op) return;
      op.rec=val; op.ho=op.rec*0.25;
    });
    D.equipes.forEach(eq=>{
      eq.rec=eq.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.rec,0);
      eq.ho=eq.ops.reduce((s,o)=>s+o.ho,0);
    });
    rebuildAll();
    refreshAll();
    localStorage.setItem('cofen_op_overrides', JSON.stringify({...local,...remote}));
    pulseSyncDot();
  });
  fbListeners.overrides = true;

  // ── Fotos ──
  fbDb.ref(fbRoom+'/photos').on('value', snap=>{
    const remote = snap.val();
    if(!remote) return;
    const local = photoGetAll();
    if(JSON.stringify(remote)===JSON.stringify(local)) return;
    localStorage.setItem('cofen_photos', JSON.stringify({...local,...remote}));
    pulseSyncDot();
  });
  fbListeners.photos = true;

  // ── Meta / Total Real Recebido ──
  fbDb.ref(fbRoom+'/meta').on('value', snap=>{
    const remote = snap.val();
    if(!remote) return;

    const remTotal = parseFloat(remote.total)||0;
    const remMeta  = parseFloat(remote.meta)||META_DEFAULT;

    // Evitar loop: só aplicar se diferente do local atual
    const localTotal = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('cofen_total'))||0;
    const localMeta  = parseFloat(localStorage.getItem('cofen_meta'))||META_DEFAULT;
    if(remTotal === localTotal && remMeta === localMeta) return;

    // Aplicar valores remotos
    if(remTotal > 0) overrideTotalRec = remTotal;
    meta = remMeta;
    localStorage.setItem('cofen_total', remTotal);
    localStorage.setItem('cofen_meta',  remMeta);

    // Atualizar input no editor se ele estiver visível
    const inpTotal = document.getElementById('inp-total');
    const inpMeta  = document.getElementById('inp-meta');
    if(inpTotal && remTotal > 0) inpTotal.value = remTotal;
    if(inpMeta)  inpMeta.value  = remMeta;

    // Recalcular e atualizar tela de todos
    refreshAll();
    pulseSyncDot();
    toast('🔄 Total atualizado em tempo real!');
  });
  fbListeners.meta = true;

  // ── Metas por Equipe ──
  fbDb.ref(fbRoom+'/metas_eq').on('value', snap=>{
    const remote = snap.val();
    if(!remote) return;
    const local = gGetMetas();
    if(JSON.stringify(remote)===JSON.stringify(local)) return;
    gSetMetas({...local,...remote});
    pulseSyncDot();
  });
  fbListeners.metas_eq = true;

  // ── Metas por Operador ──
  fbDb.ref(fbRoom+'/metas_op').on('value', snap=>{
    const remote = snap.val();
    if(!remote) return;
    const local = getMetasOp();
    if(JSON.stringify(remote)===JSON.stringify(local)) return;
    setMetasOp({...local,...remote});
    if(document.getElementById('pg-ranking')?.classList.contains('on')) mkRanking();
    pulseSyncDot();
  });
  fbListeners.metas_op = true;

  // ── Gestão (movimentação de operadores) ──
  fbDb.ref(fbRoom+'/gestao').on('value', snap=>{
    const remote = snap.val();
    if(!remote) return;
    const local = gGetOverrides();
    if(JSON.stringify(remote)===JSON.stringify(local)) return;
    gSetOverrides({...local,...remote});
    pulseSyncDot();
  });
  fbListeners.gestao = true;
}

// ── PUSH TO FIREBASE ──
function fbPush(path, data){
  if(!fbDb||!fbRoom) return;
  fbDb.ref(fbRoom+'/'+path).set(data).catch(e=>console.warn('FB push err:',e));
}

// ── PATCH LOCAL FUNCTIONS TO PUSH TO FIREBASE ──

// Patch rdSetSaved
const _rdSetSaved_fb = rdSetSaved;
function rdSetSaved(map){
  localStorage.setItem(rdTodayKey(), JSON.stringify(map));
  syncBroadcast('rd_update', JSON.stringify(map));
  fbPush('rd', map);
}

// Patch applyOps to push overrides
const _applyOps_orig = applyOps;
function applyOps(){
  _applyOps_orig();
  const ov = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('cofen_op_overrides')||'{}');
  fbPush('overrides', ov);
}

// Patch photoSet to push photos
const _photoSet_fb = photoSet;
function photoSet(opName, url){
  const all = photoGetAll();
  if(url) all[opName]=url; else delete all[opName];
  localStorage.setItem('cofen_photos', JSON.stringify(all));
  syncBroadcast('photo_update', JSON.stringify(all));
  fbPush('photos', all);
}

// ── AUTO-CONNECT FIXO — Firebase e sala já configurados ──
const FB_URL_FIXO  = 'https://cofen-dashboard-622a8-default-rtdb.firebaseio.com';
const FB_ROOM_FIXO = 'cofen-principal';

async function fbAutoConnect(){
  const url  = FB_URL_FIXO;
  const room = FB_ROOM_FIXO;
  // Salva config para o modal mostrar correto
  fbSaveCfg({url, room});
  try {
    if(!fbApp){
      fbApp = firebase.initializeApp({databaseURL: url}, 'cofen-sync-auto');
    }
    fbDb  = firebase.database(fbApp);
    fbRoom= room;
    const btn = document.getElementById('sync-topbtn');
    if(btn) btn.textContent='🔄 Sync...';
    fbStartListening();
    if(btn){ btn.textContent='🟢 Sync'; btn.style.color='var(--pp)'; btn.style.background='var(--ppl)'; }
    console.log('✅ Firebase conectado automaticamente — Sala: '+room);
  } catch(e){
    console.warn('Firebase auto-connect falhou:', e);
    const btn = document.getElementById('sync-topbtn');
    if(btn) btn.textContent='🔗 Sync';
    fbApp=null; fbDb=null; fbRoom=null;
  }
}

// ── EXPORT CSV ──
function exportCSV(){
  const rows = [
    ['Pos','Operador','Equipe','Total Real (R$)','HO 25% (R$)','Acordos Gerados','Acordos Pagos','Conversão (%)','Ticket Médio (R$)','Agendamentos']
  ];
  ALL.forEach((op,i)=>{
    const cfg = EQ[op.eq]||{sh:op.eq};
    const conv = op.gerados>0 ? (op.pagos/op.gerados*100).toFixed(1) : '0';
    rows.push([
      i+1,
      op.name.replace(/_/g,' '),
      cfg.sh,
      op.rec.toFixed(2).replace('.',','),
      op.ho.toFixed(2).replace('.',','),
      op.gerados||0,
      op.pagos||0,
      conv,
      (op.ticket||0).toFixed(2).replace('.',','),
      op.n_ag||0
    ]);
  });
  const csv = rows.map(r=>r.map(v=>'"'+String(v).replace(/"/g,'""')+'"').join(';')).join('\r\n');
  const bom = '\uFEFF'; // UTF-8 BOM para Excel
  const blob = new Blob([bom+csv],{type:'text/csv;charset=utf-8'});
  const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = url;
  const now = new Date();
  a.download = `ranking_cofen_${now.getFullYear()}${String(now.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0')}${String(now.getDate()).padStart(2,'0')}.csv`;
  a.click();
  URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
  toast('📥 CSV exportado com sucesso!');
}


// ══════════════════════════════════════════
// GESTAO DE FOTOS — ABA GESTAO > FOTOS
// ══════════════════════════════════════════
let fotosActiveEq  = 'all';
let fotosClickOp   = null;

function fotosInit(){
  const fbEl = document.getElementById('fotos-fbtns');
  if(fbEl){
    const eqs = ['all', ...D.equipes.map(e=>e.name)];
    fbEl.innerHTML = eqs.map(eq=>{
      const cfg = eq==='all' ? {sh:'Todos',c:'var(--pp)'} : (EQ[eq]||{sh:eq,c:'#888'});
      const on  = fotosActiveEq===eq;
      return '<button onclick="fotosSetEq(\'' + eq + '\')"'
        + ' style="padding:6px 14px;border-radius:var(--rm);border:1.5px solid ' + (on ? cfg.c : 'var(--g200)') + ';'
        + 'background:' + (on ? cfg.c+'18' : 'var(--w)') + ';color:' + (on ? cfg.c : 'var(--g500)') + ';'
        + 'font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;font-weight:800;font-size:11px;cursor:pointer;transition:all .2s">'
        + cfg.sh + '</button>';
    }).join('');
  }
  fotosRenderGrid();
}

function fotosSetEq(eq){
  fotosActiveEq = eq;
  fotosInit();
}

function fotosRenderGrid(){
  const grid = document.getElementById('fotos-grid');
  if(!grid) return;
  const list = fotosActiveEq==='all' ? ALL : ALL.filter(o=>o.eq===fotosActiveEq);
  const photos = photoGetAll();
  grid.innerHTML = list.map(op=>{
    const cfg     = EQ[op.eq]||{c:'#888',sh:op.eq};
    const photo   = photos[op.name];
    const hasPhoto = !!photo;
    const avatar = hasPhoto
      ? '<img src="'+photo+'" style="width:100%;height:100%;object-fit:cover;object-position:top">'
      : '<div style="width:52px;height:52px;border-radius:50%;background:'+cfg.c+';display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-weight:900;font-size:20px;color:#fff">'+ini(op.name)+'</div>';
    return '<div onclick="fotosSelectOp(\''+op.name+'\')"'
      + ' title="'+(hasPhoto?'Trocar':'Adicionar')+' foto de '+op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')+'"'
      + ' style="border-radius:var(--rl);overflow:hidden;cursor:pointer;transition:all .25s;'
      + 'border:2px solid '+(hasPhoto?cfg.c:'var(--g200)')+';position:relative;'
      + 'box-shadow:'+(hasPhoto?'0 4px 14px '+cfg.c+'33':'var(--sh)')+'"'
      + ' onmouseover="this.style.transform=\'scale(1.04)\';this.style.boxShadow=\'0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.15)\'"'
      + ' onmouseout="this.style.transform=\'\';this.style.boxShadow=\''+(hasPhoto?'0 4px 14px '+cfg.c+'33':'var(--sh)')+'\';">'
      + '<div style="height:130px;background:'+(hasPhoto?'#000':cfg.c+'18')+';display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;overflow:hidden">'
      + avatar
      + '</div>'
      + '<div style="padding:8px 10px;background:var(--w)">'
      + '<div style="font-weight:800;font-size:11px;color:var(--g900);white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis">'+op.name.replace(/_/g,' ')+'</div>'
      + '<div style="font-size:10px;color:'+cfg.c+';font-weight:700">'+cfg.sh+'</div>'
      + '<div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--g500);margin-top:2px">'+fR(op.rec)+'</div>'
      + '</div>'
      + (hasPhoto ? '<div style="position:absolute;top:6px;right:6px;background:rgba(0,0,0,.55);border-radius:100px;padding:2px 7px;font-size:9px;font-weight:700;color:#fff">✅ Foto</div>' : '')
      + '<div style="position:absolute;bottom:54px;left:0;right:0;text-align:center;background:rgba(0,0,0,.6);padding:5px 0;color:#fff;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;opacity:0;transition:opacity .2s" class="fh-lbl">'
      + (hasPhoto?'📷 Trocar foto':'📷 Adicionar foto')+'</div>'
      + '</div>';
  }).join('');

  // hover labels
  grid.querySelectorAll('div[onclick]').forEach(card=>{
    const lbl = card.querySelector('.fh-lbl');
    if(!lbl) return;
    card.addEventListener('mouseenter',()=>lbl.style.opacity='1');
    card.addEventListener('mouseleave',()=>lbl.style.opacity='0');
  });
}

function fotosSelectOp(opName){
  fotosClickOp = opName;
  const inp = document.getElementById('fotos-file-input');
  if(inp) inp.click();
}

function fotosFileSelected(inp){
  if(!inp.files||!inp.files[0]||!fotosClickOp) return;
  const file = inp.files[0];
  const reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = e => {
    photoSet(fotosClickOp, e.target.result);
    fotosRenderGrid();
    // Refresh ranking & modal if open
    if(document.getElementById('pg-ranking').classList.contains('on')) mkRanking();
    toast('✅ Foto salva para ' + fotosClickOp.replace(/_/g,' ') + '!');
    fotosClickOp = null;
  };
  reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  inp.value='';
}

// ── IMPORT UX: Drag & Drop + File Open + Clipboard ──
function impDragOver(e, dropId, color){
  e.preventDefault();
  const el = document.getElementById(dropId);
  if(el){ el.style.borderColor=color; el.style.background='rgba(0,168,107,.03)'; el.style.transform='scale(1.005)'; }
}
function impDragLeave(dropId){
  const el = document.getElementById(dropId);
  if(el){ el.style.borderColor=''; el.style.background=''; el.style.transform=''; }
}
function impDrop(e, areaId, previewFn){
  e.preventDefault();
  if(e.currentTarget && e.currentTarget.id) impDragLeave(e.currentTarget.id);
  const file = e.dataTransfer.files[0];
  if(!file) return;
  impReadFile(file, areaId, previewFn);
}
function impFileOpen(e, areaId, previewFn){
  const file = e.target.files[0];
  if(!file) return;
  impReadFile(file, areaId, previewFn);
}
function impReadFile(file, areaId, previewFn){
  const reader = new FileReader();
  reader.onload = ev => {
    const text = ev.target.result;
    const ta = document.getElementById(areaId);
    if(ta){ ta.value = text; window[previewFn](text); toast('📁 '+file.name+' carregado!'); }
  };
  reader.readAsText(file, 'UTF-8');
}
async function impPasteClipboard(areaId, previewFn){
  try {
    const text = await navigator.clipboard.readText();
    if(!text){ toast('⚠️ Área de transferência vazia'); return; }
    const ta = document.getElementById(areaId);
    if(ta){ ta.value = text; window[previewFn](text); }
    toast('📋 Colado com sucesso!');
  } catch(e){
    toast('⚠️ Permissão negada — use Ctrl+V no campo de texto');
  }
}

// ── SHOW IMPORT BADGES after successful apply ──
function markImportDone(type){
  const id = type==='rec'?'imp-rec-badge':'imp-ac-badge';
  const el = document.getElementById(id);
  if(el) el.style.display='block';
  localStorage.setItem('cofen_import_'+type+'_done','1');
}

// ── RESTORE import badges on load ──
function restoreImportBadges(){
  if(localStorage.getItem('cofen_import_rec_done')){ const b=document.getElementById('imp-rec-badge'); if(b) b.style.display='block'; }
  if(localStorage.getItem('cofen_import_ac_done')){ const b=document.getElementById('imp-ac-badge'); if(b) b.style.display='block'; }
}

// SISTEMA DE EVENTOS DO CALENDÁRIO
// ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const EV_TIPOS={
  reuniao:  {l:'Reunião',   c:'#3B82F6', bg:'#EFF6FF'},
  meta:     {l:'Meta/KPI',  c:'#00A86B', bg:'#E6F7F1'},
  feedback: {l:'Feedback',  c:'#F59E0B', bg:'#FFFBEB'},
  lembrete: {l:'Lembrete',  c:'#8B5CF6', bg:'#F5F3FF'},
  alerta:   {l:'Alerta',    c:'#EF4444', bg:'#FEF2F2'},
};

const EV_KEY='cofen_cal_events_v1';
function evGetAll(){try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(EV_KEY)||'[]');}catch{return[];}}
function evSaveAll(arr){localStorage.setItem(EV_KEY,JSON.stringify(arr));}
function evGetByDate(dateStr){return evGetAll().filter(e=>e.date===dateStr);}

let evActiveDate='';
let evEditingId=null;

function evOpenModal(dateStr){
  evActiveDate=dateStr;
  evEditingId=null;
  const evs=evGetByDate(dateStr);
  // Format date nicely
  const [y,m,d]=dateStr.split('-');
  const dt=new Date(parseInt(y),parseInt(m)-1,parseInt(d));
  const meses=['Janeiro','Fevereiro','Março','Abril','Maio','Junho','Julho','Agosto','Setembro','Outubro','Novembro','Dezembro'];
  const dias=['Domingo','Segunda','Terça','Quarta','Quinta','Sexta','Sábado'];
  const title=`📅 ${dias[dt.getDay()]}, ${d} de ${meses[parseInt(m)-1]}`;
  document.getElementById('ev-modal-date-title').textContent=title;
  document.getElementById('ev-modal-count').textContent=evs.length+' evento(s) neste dia · clique em +Novo para adicionar';
  evRenderModalBody(false);
  document.getElementById('ev-overlay').classList.add('on');
}

function evClose(){
  document.getElementById('ev-overlay').classList.remove('on');
  evEditingId=null;
}

function evRenderModalBody(showForm){
  const body=document.getElementById('ev-modal-body');
  const evs=evGetByDate(evActiveDate).sort((a,b)=>(a.hora||'').localeCompare(b.hora||''));
  let html='';

  if(showForm){
    const editing=evEditingId?evGetAll().find(e=>e.id===evEditingId):null;
    const tipoOpts=Object.entries(EV_TIPOS).map(([k,v])=>`<option value="${k}"${editing&&editing.tipo===k?' selected':''}>${v.l}</option>`).join('');
    html+=`<div style="background:var(--g50);border-radius:14px;padding:16px;border:1px solid var(--g200);margin-bottom:12px">
      <div style="font-weight:800;font-size:13px;color:var(--g900);margin-bottom:12px">${editing?'✏️ Editar Evento':'➕ Novo Evento'}</div>
      <div class="ev-form-group"><label class="ev-label">Título *</label>
        <input class="ev-inp" id="evf-titulo" value="${editing?evEsc(editing.titulo):''}" placeholder="Nome do evento, reunião, feedback..."></div>
      <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:10px">
        <div class="ev-form-group"><label class="ev-label">Tipo</label>
          <select class="ev-inp" id="evf-tipo">${tipoOpts}</select></div>
        <div class="ev-form-group"><label class="ev-label">Horário</label>
          <input class="ev-inp" type="time" id="evf-hora" value="${editing&&editing.hora?editing.hora:''}"></div>
      </div>
      <div class="ev-form-group"><label class="ev-label">Descrição / Notas</label>
        <textarea class="ev-inp" id="evf-desc" placeholder="Detalhes, pontos discutidos, decisões...">${editing&&editing.descricao?evEsc(editing.descricao):''}</textarea></div>
      <div class="ev-form-group"><label class="ev-label">🔔 Lembrete / Alerta</label>
        <input class="ev-inp" id="evf-lembrete" value="${editing&&editing.lembrete?evEsc(editing.lembrete):''}" placeholder="Ex: Ligar para equipe, enviar relatório..."></div>
      <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:4px">
        <button onclick="${editing?'evUpdate()':'evSave()'}"
          style="flex:1;padding:10px;border-radius:var(--rm);border:none;cursor:pointer;
          background:linear-gradient(135deg,var(--pp),var(--pp3));color:#fff;
          font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;font-weight:800;font-size:13px">
          💾 ${editing?'Salvar Alterações':'Cadastrar Evento'}
        </button>
        <button onclick="evRenderModalBody(false)"
          style="padding:10px 16px;border-radius:var(--rm);border:1.5px solid var(--g200);
          background:var(--w);color:var(--g700);font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;font-weight:700;font-size:12px;cursor:pointer">
          Cancelar
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  }

  if(evs.length===0 && !showForm){
    html+=`<div style="text-align:center;padding:24px 0;color:var(--g500);font-size:12px;font-weight:600">
      Nenhum evento neste dia.<br>
      <button onclick="evShowForm()"
        style="margin-top:10px;padding:8px 18px;border-radius:var(--rm);border:none;cursor:pointer;
        background:linear-gradient(135deg,var(--pp),var(--pp3));color:#fff;
        font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;font-weight:800;font-size:12px">
        + Criar Primeiro Evento
      </button>
    </div>`;
  }

  evs.forEach(ev=>{
    const cfg=EV_TIPOS[ev.tipo]||EV_TIPOS.lembrete;
    html+=`<div class="ev-item-card" style="background:${cfg.bg};border:1.5px solid ${cfg.c}33;margin-bottom:8px">
      <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;gap:10px">
        <div style="width:10px;height:10px;border-radius:50%;background:${cfg.c};margin-top:3px;flex-shrink:0"></div>
        <div style="flex:1;min-width:0">
          <div style="font-weight:900;font-size:13px;color:var(--g900)">${evEsc(ev.titulo)}</div>
          <div style="display:flex;gap:6px;margin-top:4px;flex-wrap:wrap;align-items:center">
            <span style="background:${cfg.c};color:#fff;padding:2px 8px;border-radius:100px;font-size:10px;font-weight:800">${cfg.l}</span>
            ${ev.hora?`<span style="background:var(--g100);color:var(--g700);padding:2px 8px;border-radius:100px;font-size:10px;font-weight:700">🕐 ${ev.hora}</span>`:''}
          </div>
          ${ev.descricao?`<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--g700);font-weight:600;margin-top:7px;line-height:1.55">${evEsc(ev.descricao).replace(/\n/g,'<br>')}</div>`:''}
          ${ev.lembrete?`<div style="font-size:11px;color:#92400E;font-weight:700;background:#FEF3C7;border-radius:6px;padding:4px 9px;display:inline-block;margin-top:6px">🔔 ${evEsc(ev.lembrete)}</div>`:''}
          <div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--g300);margin-top:6px">Compartilhado · ID: ${ev.id}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="display:flex;gap:4px;flex-shrink:0">
          <button onclick="evStartEdit('${ev.id}')"
            style="padding:5px 9px;border-radius:var(--r);border:1.5px solid var(--g200);
            background:var(--w);color:var(--g700);cursor:pointer;font-size:11px;font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;font-weight:700">✏️</button>
          <button onclick="evDelete('${ev.id}')"
            style="padding:5px 9px;border-radius:var(--r);border:1.5px solid #FCA5A5;
            background:var(--w);color:var(--danger);cursor:pointer;font-size:11px;font-family:Nunito,sans-serif;font-weight:700">🗑</button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  });

  body.innerHTML=html;
}

function evEsc(s){return (s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');}

function evShowForm(){evEditingId=null;evRenderModalBody(true);}

function evStartEdit(id){
  evEditingId=id;
  evRenderModalBody(true);
}

function evSave(){
  const titulo=(document.getElementById('evf-titulo')?.value||'').trim();
  if(!titulo){toast('⚠️ Título é obrigatório');return;}
  const ev={
    id:Date.now().toString()+Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,6),
    date:evActiveDate,
    titulo,
    tipo:document.getElementById('evf-tipo')?.value||'lembrete',
    hora:document.getElementById('evf-hora')?.value||'',
    descricao:document.getElementById('evf-desc')?.value||'',
    lembrete:document.getElementById('evf-lembrete')?.value||'',
    criadoEm:new Date().toISOString()
  };
  const all=evGetAll();
  all.push(ev);
  evSaveAll(all);
  evRenderModalBody(false);
  // Atualiza calendários
  buildCal('cal-grid'); buildCal('cal-grid2');
  toast('📅 Evento salvo!');
  // BroadcastChannel sync
  try{ if(typeof rdBC!=='undefined')rdBC.postMessage({type:'cal_event',data:ev});}catch{}
}

function evUpdate(){
  const titulo=(document.getElementById('evf-titulo')?.value||'').trim();
  if(!titulo){toast('⚠️ Título é obrigatório');return;}
  const all=evGetAll();
  const idx=all.findIndex(e=>e.id===evEditingId);
  if(idx===-1){toast('Evento não encontrado');return;}
  all[idx]={...all[idx],titulo,
    tipo:document.getElementById('evf-tipo')?.value||'lembrete',
    hora:document.getElementById('evf-hora')?.value||'',
    descricao:document.getElementById('evf-desc')?.value||'',
    lembrete:document.getElementById('evf-lembrete')?.value||''
  };
  evSaveAll(all);
  evEditingId=null;
  evRenderModalBody(false);
  buildCal('cal-grid'); buildCal('cal-grid2');
  toast('✏️ Evento atualizado!');
}

function evDelete(id){
  if(!confirm('Remover este evento?')) return;
  evSaveAll(evGetAll().filter(e=>e.id!==id));
  evRenderModalBody(false);
  buildCal('cal-grid'); buildCal('cal-grid2');
  toast('🗑 Evento removido');
}

// Refresh calendars every 30s to pick up changes from other tabs
setInterval(()=>{
  buildCal('cal-grid');
  buildCal('cal-grid2');
}, 30000);

</script>
